Public Telegram

Deng Xihou sends a telegram to the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, Chairman Lin of the National Government, Ministers of various Yuan, Nanchang Chairman Jiang Junjian, Provincial Governments of various provinces, General Commanders of various routes, Army Commanders of various armies, Party Headquarters at all levels, Chongqing Supervisor Liu, Division Commander Ji, Division Commander Luo, Suiding Army Commander Liu, Guang'an Army Commander Yang, Tongchuan Supervisor Tian, Brigade Commanders of various divisions, Commanders of various units, County Magistrates of various counties, various agencies and legal entities, and various newspapers:

I, Xihou, received a telegram from Chairman Jiang during the winter, instructing me to assist in suppressing the Red bandits and avoid repeating the mistakes of Hubei and Jiangxi. I followed the order and left the province on a certain date, personally inspecting the troops in the garrison area to make selections. I have already reported these matters separately. Later, upon arriving in Xindu, I received another telegram from the Chairman on the 30th, instructing that units that have not participated in the bandit suppression should be quickly selected to reinforce the five provinces. It is inappropriate to take advantage of the situation to occupy defensive positions and cause internal strife, creating opportunities for the bandits.

I, Xihou, strictly followed the telegram's instructions and was in the midst of inspecting and selecting troops in Xindu when I suddenly received a report from the troops stationed in Wenjiang that Liu Wenhui, the army commander of the 24th Army, had dispatched troops in two directions to pressure Wenjiang on a certain day. I ordered them to retreat to avoid war. On another day, they forced our troops stationed in Jianyang to leave the city and occupied it exclusively. In recent days, they have further forcibly occupied our Chengdu tax collection agencies, an endless and aggressive grab.

I, Xihou, while retreating, still made efforts to mediate and sent a telegram to the Central Government to stop them and order them to reflect. However, Liu Wenhui has no remorse and on the first day of the year, he divided his troops into four routes and launched a major attack on our Peng, Guan, Xindu, Jintang, and Ziyang counties. This is taking an inch and demanding a yard, and retreat is no longer possible.

Considering that the Communist bandits are rampant and spreading in Sichuan, causing concern in the Central Government, which has repeatedly ordered that there should be no distinction in territory and that troops should be dispatched to assist in suppressing the bandits, I, Xihou, had just begun selecting troops when Liu Wenhui repeatedly started conflicts with me, seemingly deliberately echoing the Red bandits, preventing me, Xihou, from participating in the bandit suppression work. This is in direct contradiction to Chairman Jiang's repeated telegrams not to occupy defensive positions and cause internal strife.

It is unbelievable that Liu Wenhui, holding the position of chairman, has shown no achievement in governance and has created obstacles in bandit suppression, disregarding what is right, undermining the Sichuan situation, and being heartless and unjust to this extent. It is truly lamentable.

I believe that the turmoil in Sichuan cannot be resolved by military force, as the Central Government has already declared and the people have appealed. This sentiment and reason are shared by the entire nation. The sacrifices in last year's battles were greater than in the past, but what was gained in return? At a time when the wounds have not yet healed, the violent Japanese are approaching Tianjin and the Red bandits are still harassing the northern routes. Even striving for relief is barely enough. If we still act recklessly and start wars, what is the point?

If there is still a glimmer of hope and a shred of conscience, how can one bear to do this? If we disregard national difficulties and common suffering, and instead engage in petty squabbles and ruthless abuse of the people, then even though I, Xihou, love peace and can endure humiliation, it is difficult to suppress the anger of my subordinates and prevent legitimate defense.

I request the Central Government to uphold the law and maintain justice, severely punishing Liu Wenhui for starting a war and ruining the region without cause. I also hope that all gentlemen will uphold justice and speak out, restraining tyranny so that those who love to create chaos will be warned and the bandit suppression work can proceed. I anxiously await your orders.

Deng Xihou, Army Commander of the 28th Army of the National Revolutionary Army and concurrently General Commander of the 14th Route, bows in respect.

The League of Nations Special Committee Secretly Discusses the Bolivia-Paraguay Dispute

Paraguayan Military Announces War Report

Bolivian Planes Conduct Heavy Bombing

▲ Reuters, Geneva, 15th - The special committee of the League of Nations Administrative Council dealing with the conflict between Paraguay and Bolivia held a secret meeting today to discuss the conflict between the two countries. The committee wants to prepare recommendations to submit to the next meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council. It is reported that today, methods of sending a fact-finding mission and seeking arbitration to stop the war were discussed.

▲ Havas News Agency, Asuncion, Paraguay, 15th - The Ministry of the Army announced that a detachment of the 36th Infantry Regiment of the Bolivian Army was mostly killed by Paraguayan troops in the Sandino war zone, leaving over a hundred bodies. Three Bolivian officers were killed and the rest were captured. The Paraguayan army also seized a large amount of war loot.

▲ Havas News Agency, Buenos Aires, Argentina, 16th - The owner of the Bugasa factory in Paraguay arrived here yesterday and claimed that Bolivian planes bombed the factory, killing many workers, including women and children. He has closed the factory and laid off 2,000 workers. It is reported that the Bolivian aircrews, hired by German consultant General Gentel, are all Swiss and German nationals.

Germany Protests to Austria

▲ National News Agency, Berlin, 15th - The German Minister to Vienna has been instructed by the German government to submit a note to the Austrian government, protesting the fact that the Vienna Police Commissioner, representing the Austrian government, did not welcome the German cabinet ministers who arrived at the Austrian airport in Aspern last Saturday. This matter has caused a great uproar in German public opinion, which feels that the Austrian government should not violate its friendly policy towards Germany and treat the important members of the German government who came to Austria to attend a legal conference with disrespect.

▲ National News Agency, Vienna, 16th - The Executive Committee of the Austrian Christian Social Party has resolved to recognize Hitler as the supreme leader of all Germany and to join the Austrian Social Democratic Party and a certain group in Styria in forming a new fighting front. Some say that this decision will shake the Dolfuss government. On Sunday, National Socialists demonstrated throughout the country and clashed with the Heimwehr, resulting in a total of 2,334 arrests, many of whom were Germans. Most of those arrested were released after paying fines, with only 300 still in custody awaiting trial. Fifty-four German students in Innsbruck participated in the demonstrations and have been ordered by local officials to leave Austria within 24 hours.

France Woos Turkey

▲ National News Agency, Paris, 15th - In order to implement its economic diplomacy policy and manipulate international politics using state funds, France has decided to lend a large sum of money to Turkey. According to the influential industrial organization "Le Journée Industrielle", French financial groups plan to lend the Turkish government 600 million or 500 million Turkish pounds at a very low interest rate and with a very long repayment period, so that Turkey can use this large sum of money to revitalize its domestic industry and purchase railway materials and military supplies from France.

American Striking Farmers Publicly Fight with Police

Using Bricks and Stones as Weapons

Tear Gas Ineffective

Forcefully Occupy Pundor Town

▲ National News Agency, Milwaukee, 15th - American striking farmers openly fought with state police today in the Green Bay area, one hundred miles north of here. According to the latest news, the farmers were victorious and occupied the small town of Pundor. Initially, about 1,000 striking farmers guarded the main roads outside Pundor, intercepting vehicles and trains transporting agricultural products. If the drivers resisted, they were dragged to nearby fields and guarded.

Minutes after the incident, tax collectors and road police arrived and fired tear gas bombs, but the farmers had already brought bricks and stones in their cars. Bricks and pointed sticks flew at the police, who were unable to resist and were forced to retreat. The farmers then destroyed the milk and dairy products in the vehicles, swarmed into the town, beat up councilors, and occupied the entire town.

Most retail stores are now closed, but the strikers are still swarming into creameries, smashing their vats and pouring the finished goods into the streets. Factory employees were unable to stop them because the strikers had sent pickets into the city in advance to investigate places storing large quantities of butter and cheese. Therefore, places with more inventory were destroyed today, and places with less inventory were not invaded, but deliveries were also prohibited. Local merchants have urgently telegraphed Madison City, requesting the authorities to quickly send state troops to suppress the unrest.

Notes from the War Zone

Special Correspondent Geng Ya of This Newspaper

(Defensive Engineering Abandoned Like Worn-Out Shoes)

(The Enemy's Means Are Insidious and Despicable)

Guye Special Dispatch. The Japanese, in order to satisfy their aggressive ambitions of "not giving up until they reach the Yellow River," have repeatedly used their familiar trick of deceiving themselves and others, and at the beginning of the month, they fabricated excuses to confuse the international community. On the 7th, they restarted the Luan River incident, suddenly capturing the counties and towns of Funing, Shuangwangbao, Lulong, and Qian'an on the eastern section of the Pingyu Avenue. Along the Beining Railway, they also occupied Beidaihe, Liushouying, and Changli, and even advanced to the positions of Anshan, Jingjiadianzi, Liguan, and Shimen stations.

Yesterday, the bad news spread that the enemy had forcibly crossed the Luan River and broken through the Gaotaizi defense line of Commander Song’s army, extending over two hundred li. A certain place west of the Luan River on the left wing of Commander He’s army was in danger of being encircled by the enemy. Senior officers of the army headquarters immediately held an emergency meeting to discuss countermeasures.

At 7 p.m., I visited Army Commander He Zhuguo, who said, "The Japanese are so rampant. If the country does not coordinate measures, the future is very dangerous. The key areas of Xifengkou and Gubeikou, which we are now defending, are extremely important. If anything unexpected happens again, Tianjin will have no defenses to rely on." He also gave me two photos of shot-down Japanese planes.

Then, I visited Hong Sheng, the magistrate of Luan County, and inquired about the people's situation after the county fell into the war zone. After saying goodbye, it was already 9 p.m. When I returned, I saw a service member from the adjutant's office packing boxes and luggage. Surprised, I asked, and learned that the army headquarters was about to move to a certain place. I also hastily left the city. The moonlight was bleak, and I felt gloomy. Modern women, petite and exquisite, were hurrying along the sandy path, accompanied by soldiers carrying boxes and bags. I guessed they were the families of officers, but I couldn't be sure.

After arriving at the station and waiting for a while, the train arrived and we eagerly boarded. The train had no roof, so I looked up at the stars and moon and down at the people. The sights and sounds from the front line came flooding into my mind. I remember when I rode with the propaganda team along the Luan River defense line to give speeches in various villages, I saw that our riverfront positions were quite strong, but because they had not been repaired for a long time, the wooden frames had sprouted and branched out, and the trenches were filled with wind and sand.

As the train started, it traveled north over the Luan River railway bridge. The peaks turned and the road twisted. Above were hanging cliffs, and below was the Luan River. The scenery was serene. The Qianlong Imperial Palace was in sight. When we arrived at Liugezhuang, the propaganda team members gave speeches everywhere. I happened to meet a platoon leader who had just withdrawn from the front line to defend this place.

He said that the positions and bunkers built by our army in Shimenzhai, Haiyangzhen, Qinhuangdao, Niutouguan, Liujiang, and other places were strongly built with lime, fine stone, and huge timber, and strengthened with barbed wire and various obstacles, costing three or four hundred thousand yuan. The cost of the timber was not included. It was very difficult to build during the severe cold. It was hard to dig into the frozen ground even an inch. We painstakingly built these defenses, originally intending to defend them to the death, but when Lengkou fell, an order came out and we retreated. The positions created with blood, sweat, and money were mostly not reused and abandoned like worn-out shoes. This is extremely painful.

After the non-resistance general stepped down and the superiors changed, our soldiers all rejoiced and said that the opportunity to bravely kill the enemy had arrived. However, the enemy restarted the conflict this time, and our soldiers were sharpening their fists and vowing to fight to the death. As a result, their hearts and wishes were betrayed. Unfortunately, we were born as Chinese, and even more unfortunately, we were born as anti-Japanese soldiers in name only. The words "deeply sinful" on the obituary are a portrayal of the dilemma faced by our soldiers today.

A sergeant major even said frankly, "Let's be honest, brothers. Given the current situation, if it weren't for the external enemy, there would be many mutinies." I could only offer a wry smile, as I had no words of comfort. At the same time, a question that had been hanging in my mind for a long time was finally resolved by their words. The rapid advance of the Japanese army has a reason.

An old village chief from Hanjiazhuang in ten townships of Lulong County said, "An army that can fight bravely will definitely not harass the people. Conversely, an army that harasses the people everywhere cannot fight. China has been in civil war for years, causing great suffering to the people. In addition, after the September 18th Incident, the residents in the war zone have supplied military needs, which has mostly exceeded their ability to bear. If they are harassed by illegal soldiers again, they can only resign themselves to being slaves of a conquered country, because the crime is nothing more than that."

Army Commander He understood the people's difficulties and sent out secret agents. Illegal soldiers were punished by military law if they were discovered or reported. The people were very grateful. In the villages I visited, most of the residents had fled, and well-off families had mostly fled to the mining areas. The rest either stayed behind or took temporary refuge in the mountains and cellars. Luan City was once completely empty, but after the county magistrate and army personnel went to persuade them, some gradually returned to cultivate the land. However, how long did it last before they suffered the tragedy of fleeing again?

Luan County has a vast area and a population of over 910,000. Last year, it collected enough 70,000 in land tax and grain. It has strived to develop education, but most of the schools in the city and near the river have been dissolved in name. The graduation exams were held in Tangshan. Superstition is still prevalent in the countryside, and it has not been broken. The "Zhang Tianshi enters Beijing, and half the people will die this year" warning is diligently copied and circulated, and it is everywhere. The morale of the people seems quite low, but the workers in the mining area and the nearby residents have a vigorous spirit. The county militia of about 3,000 men can still fulfill their responsibility to maintain law and order. The prisoners in custody had already been sent to Tianjin, but when Changli and other counties were about to fall, they sent another 130 people. When they were transferred to Tianjin, they were rejected. Keeping them meant no food for the prisoners, and releasing them meant no authority. Officials like to shirk their responsibilities to each other, which can be seen from this. What is suffering is only this group of prisoners.

Wherever the enemy army goes, if they ask for something from the people, they must first bow deeply. When drinking water, they must also feign to offer a 1-mao coin in order to deceive our villagers. The leaflets distributed by the planes have absurd words on one side and seductive erotic pictures on the other. The intention is insidious and the methods are despicable. (13th)

The Sichuan War Situation Expands

The 29th Army Also Joins the Battle, Disturbing the Entire Province. Fierce Fighting on Both Sides in the Jianyang Area Causes Many Casualties. Jiang Sends Telegram to Cease Fire to Avoid Creating Opportunities for the Communist Bandits

Chongqing Correspondence: The Sichuan war has officially broken out again. The 24th and 28th armies are now in a period of fierce fighting. Deng Jinkang, the army commander of the 28th Army, left Chengdu on the 4th and went to Xindu, where he was stationed in Baoguang Temple, directing military operations in all directions. He planned to concentrate in three routes: one to Xindu and Hanzhou, one to Pixian and Guanxian, and one to Jianyang and Lezhi. He appointed three route commanders: Chen Shunu, the commander of the 3rd Division, as the commander of the first route; Huang Yimin, the commander of the 2nd Division, as the commander of the second route; and Yang Rongxiang, the commander of the Training Division, as the commander of the third route. Each was assigned a force of over 15,000 men, deployed in front of the battle line, to fight the 24th Army.

Expanding the Front

Liu Zigan of the 24th Army had made full preparations for the battle. He appointed Wang Yuanhu, the commander of the 5th Division, as the commander-in-chief of the first route, leading 20,000 troops to attack Wenjiang, Pixian, and Guanxian, which became the fuse. He used the 22,000 troops of Chen Hongwen's 6th Division to press on Jianyang, with Chen as the commander-in-chief of the second route. He used Zhang Zhihe's 1st Division, leading 30,000 troops, to advance from Chengdu to the Xinhu-Hanzhong area, with Zhang as the commander-in-chief of the third route.

After both sides deployed their forces, on the 5th, Wang Yuanhu's troops clashed with the Zhou Shaozhi Brigade of the 28th Army stationed in Shiyangchang, which belongs to Chongqing, followed by fierce fighting. The sound of gunfire for three hours shattered the calm Sichuan situation. This was the opening ceremony of the Sichuan war again. On the 6th, both sides mobilized their troops more urgently, preparing for a major battle. On the 7th, the major battle began. Wang Yuanhu used five regiments to engage the Zhou Shaozhi Brigade of the 28th Army stationed in Wenjiang, followed by hand-to-hand combat. Zhou was unable to withstand it and abandoned Wenjiang, and the 24th Army immediately moved into the area. Liu Zigan then used 50,000 troops to put general pressure on Xindu, Hanzhou, Pixian, and Guanxian, wanting to drive the 28th Army into the Songli Mao area and occupy their territory.

On the 8th, the Baoding-affiliated generals and officers in the 24th and 28th armies came forward again as Lu Zhonglian, making every effort to mediate in the hope of shortening the front and preventing the war from expanding. However, their efforts were unsuccessful.

Disturbing the Entire Province

On the 10th, the war clouds were dense and the atmosphere became tense again. On the night of the 11th, fierce fighting broke out in the Jianyang area. Chen Hongwen used ten regiments to attack the county seat. After Chen Shunu's troops, You Guangju, and Sun Xiansong's brigades calmly responded, Wang Xuejiang's brigade launched a surprise attack, defeating Chen Hongwen's troops. Both sides suffered more than a thousand casualties. On the 12th, Liu Zigan increased reinforcements by mobilizing the Shi Zhaowu and Mou Suifang brigades to besiege Jianyang and attack Lezhi directly.

On the 13th, another fierce battle broke out. Chen Shunu's troops were weak and in danger of collapse, but they had made contact with Li Qixiang of the New 6th Division stationed in Anyue Suining. If necessary, Li could participate in the war and confront the 24th Army. The troops of the 29th Army stationed in the Shehong area were also preparing to assist the 28th Army. The Red bandits who fled to Sichuan, in order to promote the outbreak of the Sichuan war, abandoned Tongjiang, Nanjiang, Bazhong, and other places, and made other plans to allow the Sichuan warlords to recklessly fight each other in order to reap the benefits of watching from the sidelines. Therefore, the 29th Army had the opportunity to participate in the civil war, acting in concert with Deng Jinkang to resist the invasion of the 24th Army.

On the afternoon of the 13th, fierce fighting broke out in Xindu, Guanxian, and Pixian between the 24th and 28th armies. Deng Jinkang personally commanded the military operations in the army. Neither side prevailed.

Declaring Their Position

Deng then sent a telegram to the entire Sichuan province, declaring that the re-opening of the Sichuan war was purely due to the 24th Army provoking a dispute and bullying friendly troops. During this period of serious national crisis, they were committing such a rebellious act. He asked all parties to uphold justice and support each other with righteousness. Tian Songyao of the 29th Army also sent a telegram to all parties, saying that Liu took advantage of the fact that the Red bandits in northern Sichuan had not yet been suppressed and擅自啓 川戰 端, creating an opportunity for the Communist Party. Sending troops to press on Jinkang was no different from demonstrating to the 29th Army. In addition to participating with the entire army and making righteous efforts, he would also open up routes and lead them into the 24th Army's defense zone, disrupting their various activities to punish their nature of loving chaos.

Liu Zigan also sent a telegram to all parties, saying that since the previous war, the army's defense area had shrunk and the troops could not be maintained. Rather than sitting and waiting to die, it would be better to open up a way out, temporarily borrowing friendly troops' defense areas to temporarily solve the current difficulties and maintain the status quo.

Yang Sen of the 20th Army stationed in the north and Liu Cunhou of the 23rd Army stationed in Suiding issued a telegram expressing their attitude towards the dispute between Deng and Liu, requesting that military action be stopped immediately and that both sides守著陣線静候 中央 裁决, not to轻啓衅端, causing suffering to the people of Sichuan and disturbing the various armies.

However, Liu Xiang of the 21st Army stationed in southeastern Sichuan has an ambiguous and unclear attitude, expressing no support for any party. It is rumored that the reason why Liu Zigan dared to send troops to press on the 28th Army was that he had obtained Liu Xiang's consent in advance. Because Liu Zigan and Liu Xiang are uncle and nephew. In the previous war, Liu Xiang seized more than four counties from Liu Zigan's defense area, and they were all fertile land, making it difficult for the army to maintain itself. Therefore, Liu Xiang tacitly allowed him to develop in other directions without interfering, so there was no clear attitude. Now, even though the great war between the Liu and Deng armies has begun, there is no expression of any kind.

Jiang's Telegram to Cease Fire

Chairman Jiang of the Military Commission sent a telegram a few days ago to stop the Sichuan war. The original telegram said, "Limited to arrival immediately, Chongqing Supervisor Liu Fu Cheng brother, San-tai Supervisor Tian Song-yao brother, Chengdu General Commander Liu Zi Gan brother, Deng Army Commander Jin Kang brother, Suining Yang Army Commander Zi Hui brother, Sui-ding Liu Army Commander Ji Zhi brother and transfer to each division commander,The Sichuan Red bandit encirclement plan was negotiated by the headquarters sending liaison staff Yin Zuchun, Ye Wei, etc. to Sichuan, to consult with Brother Songyao and the representatives sent by Fu Cheng to jointly formulate it. It is still appropriate. Now I hear that Tian's troops have recovered Tongjiang, if each unit can advance at the same time and attack from different directions, then the Communist bandits will not be able to take care of both ends and will not have time to reorganize. It will not be difficult to sweep them away in one fell swoop. The key to the problem is that we must have the determination to have no bandits or me and strive for the real effect of working together. Material replenishment, mutual accommodation and whether there is or is not, still no self-dividing territories, or slightly hesitant, each unit based on the plan, rectify the troops, urgent advance and urgent attack, all the troops that have not participated in the encirclement of the red bandits, should be drawn urgently, mutual support, Wan should not take advantage of the opportunity to resist the virtual, invade the defense area, self-start internal struggle, so as to avoid creating opportunities for the communist bandits. The Xu Kuang remnant troops entered Sichuan at the beginning, not more than ten thousand people, without being severely suppressed at the beginning, so that they were fortified in Tongjiang, the bandit troops threatened the masses everywhere, the harm became more and more profound, relying on deep and thick, will inevitably spread, more difficult to clean up than the situation in Gan and E. The failure of Gan and E, there are many precedents, enough to be a lesson, I hope that you brothers will join forces and abandon resentment, stop internal struggle, and do not make a big mistake for luck. All the circumstances of the meeting and advance encirclement, I hope to report at any time. Zhong Zheng seal."

Since the Liu and Deng armies fought each other, all the celebrities and important figures from all walks of life in Sichuan, such as Yin Changheng, Xu Xiaogang, Zhou Dao, Xu Jiong, and Chen Guodong, also sent telegrams asking to stop the civil war and not to suffer the people of Sichuan again. (15th)

The Nineteenth Route Army's Anti-Japanese Vanguard's Itinerary

(Will pass through Hunan Province and head directly to Wuhan, then north)

Guangzhou News: The two detachments of the Nineteenth Route Army's Anti-Japanese Vanguard that arrived in Guangdong, after reaching Yuantan and being inspected and addressed by Cai Tingkai, the first detachment continued its advance towards Shaoguan from Yuantan on the 8th of this month. Yang Hanzong's and Xie Dingxin's regiments of this detachment arrived in Lechang late on the night of the 11th. The two regimental commanders, Yang and Xie, and the political training personnel of the regiment, immediately convened local groups, detailing the significance of passing through the north, so people along the way welcomed them sincerely. As for the second detachment, Wu Luxun's and Yang Changhuang's regiments, they are expected to assemble in Lechang on the 12th, and together advance to Pingshi, passing through Hunan Province and heading directly to Wuhan. As for the first and second detachment commanders, Zhang Yan and Tan Qixiu, they are scheduled to depart from Guangzhou today (12th) with Shen Chongxi, the director of the campaign headquarters, and all the personnel of the headquarters, heading north. In addition, Chen Fuyuan, the director of the military supply department of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, has been approved by Commander-in-Chief Cai to come to Guangdong and accompany the Anti-Japanese Vanguard north to fight the enemy. This time, the Nineteenth Route Army's Anti-Japanese Vanguard, in addition to the four regiments of troops, also has a Youth Service Corps, all organized by patriotic volunteers who aspire to serve the country by joining the army. The corps commander is Jin Yiting, the deputy commander is Zheng Jiannan, and it has internal advisors, a propaganda section, a general affairs section, a medical aid section, an administrative unit, a photography unit, a drawing unit, a lecture unit, a secretariat, special agents, a resident Guangdong commissioner, and a resident Hong Kong commissioner, etc. The corps is now departing in two batches, the first batch has already arrived in Shaoguan Lechang with the army, and the second batch departs today with the campaign headquarters. Yesterday, a public telegram was issued, saying, "1. (Omitted honorary titles) The brutal Japanese are bullying us to this extreme, having occupied our eastern provinces and captured Rehe and Yu, encroaching upon our territory by the day, threatening the very existence of our nation. The loyal and brave Nineteenth Route Army, revered by all, has risen in righteous resistance, sending an advance force to aid Rehe. The youth of Guangdong, stirred by righteous indignation, have voluntarily organized a service corps. The first detachment is heading north, vowing to annihilate the enemy with their blood and heads. Their journey is underway, and they will not turn back. We hope that all our comrades will rise up together. May those of understanding throughout the country teach them and guide them, and we shall be fortunate. Jin Yiting, Commander of the Youth Military Service Corps, Deputy Commanders Zheng Jiannan and Chen Shangxiong, lead all corps members in bowing." After the Guangdong Youth Service Corps set off, more than forty patriotic youths from Shanghai joined the corps. After approval by Commander-in-Chief Cai Tingkai, the corps commander, Jin Yiting, considering that the army was already passing through Hunan Province to Wuhan, and to avoid circuitous routes, ordered the Shanghai service corps to go directly to Wuhan from Shanghai to await assembly. A telegram was sent to Shanghai on the 11th to inform the personnel. Chen Mingshu, after arriving in Guangdong for many days and meeting with various parties, took the Jinshan vessel to Hong Kong from Guangzhou at 8:00 AM on the 11th, accompanied by his wife Zhu Guangzhen and Ouyang Ju, etc. Many military and political figures came to see him off. According to Chen, the impression he gained from this return to Guangdong was very good. After arriving in Hong Kong, he will go to Fujian or inspect the military situation at the front lines in Beiping and Tianjin, but nothing has been decided yet. As for Cai Tingkai, the commander-in-chief of the Nineteenth Route Army, he still needs to stay in Guangdong for a few days to handle the affairs of the Anti-Japanese Vanguard heading north before returning to Fujian. (12th)

Fengxian

Order to Implement Education for Prisoners

The county government received an order from the provincial government yesterday, instructing it to immediately set up education for prisoners, establish a repentance room, and recommend several repentance teachers to take turns visiting the prison to implement repentance education, hoping to achieve the effect of reforming prisoners and turning them to good. Currently, the county government has instructed the Education Bureau to instruct the two civil education centers of Nanqiao and Fengcheng to send personnel to the prisons on a monthly basis to implement repentance education.

Songjiang

Telegram Requesting Completion

of the Puhuitang Project

The Sijing Town Chamber of Commerce believes that the Puhuitang River has been dredged in various sections of Songjiang and Qingpu, but the section from Yaotianqiao Daigang west to Tushanwan has not yet started construction, which is of great importance to inland transportation. Yesterday, they specifically telegraphed Shanghai Mayor Wu to order the bureau to dredge it. The original telegram said, "To Mayor Wu Jun of Shanghai: We have found that the Puhuitang River is an important waterway for the towns of Xujiahui, Hongqiao, Qibao, Sijing, Qingpu, and Songjiang in Shanghai. Due to years of neglect, it has become silted up and shallow. The people along the river have repeatedly appealed, and finally the National Government's Songhu War Zone Relief Association allocated funds for dredging. Now, various sections have been gradually put into construction, and the Songqing River section has been completed. The local people are deeply gratified. However, the section from Tianyao Bridge Daigang west to Tushanwan has not yet started construction, which is incomprehensible. We have found that this section is the head of the entire river and is of great importance to the commercial transportation of the towns along the river. Moreover, we have found that the Relief Association's allocation of funds for this section is also included in the plan. Now that various sections are about to be completed, only this section has been delayed, which is deeply feared to affect inland transportation. Therefore, we telegraphically request that you order the Public Works Bureau to urgently excavate this section of the river, so that the entire river will be uniformly deep and facilitate inland commercial transportation."

Suzhou

Cook Stabs Housewife to Death

Yang Shaoliang, who once served as the section chief of the Third Section of the Suzhou Police Affairs on the Jinghu Road, a native of Shou County, Anhui, rented a house at No. 15 Sibaidu Guan Lane near the Suzhou Station while in office and lived there with his family. After leaving office, he still lived in the original place. He had three wives and concubines. His second concubine, Ms. Yuan, 41 years old, a native of Changzhou, was suddenly stabbed to death in her room at 3:00 AM on the 16th. She was stabbed once in the chest with a small knife. It was heard that after Ms. Yuan was stabbed, she still got up to chase the murderer, but fell to the ground and died after walking a few steps. After the case occurred, Xu Dianchen, a native of Shou County who provided meals at his home, disappeared. He was subsequently captured by detective Yang Fushan at Huguan and sent to the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau for interrogation on the morning of the same day.

Taicang

Director of National Goods Exhibition Under Surveillance

The Shanghai National Goods Traveling Troupe, under the pretext of exhibiting national goods, mixed in and sold Japanese goods. This was discovered and reported by citizens Lu Zuheng and Zhang Menghua, and confirmed by the Hate Goods Inspection Association. It is now learned that the county party headquarters held a meeting the night before last and decided to notify the county government to temporarily place the person in charge under surveillance and telegraph the province to ask for instructions on how to deal with the matter. They also telegraphed the county government yesterday, requesting that the bailiffs temporarily place Wang Yanqing, the person in charge of the troupe, under surveillance pending resolution.

Wuxi

Gangsters Extort Watch Shop

Zhu Baochang Watch Shop on Shengxiang Bridge Street in the city, opened by Zhu Fengzao, a native of the county. The other day, Zhu's wife suddenly received a threatening letter from a gangster, signed "Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps," demanding 1,000 yuan, and agreeing to meet at Seventy-Two Rocking Car Bay in Huishan on the twentieth day of the old calendar, and hand it over to someone wearing a duckbill hat and a short coat, otherwise, don't blame our country for its ruthless methods, etc. Zhu's wife was greatly frightened after receiving the letter, but decided to ignore it because business in the store was slow and there was no such large sum of money at the moment.

Municipal Engineering Taken Over by the County

The First District Office of this county, because municipal engineering belongs to the scope of the First District, specifically requested the county government to forward a request to the Construction Department, asking that the affairs of the municipal engineering office of this county be transferred to the District Office for handling. In addition, citizens Cao Quan and others also jointly submitted a request to the Construction Department, exhaustively stating the reasons for changing the system of the municipal engineering under the jurisdiction of the county government's technical office. After receiving the submission, the Construction Department believed that the municipal engineering office was responsible for undertakings that were mostly technical and sanitary in scope, and that specialized personnel were required for its design and construction. The temporary cancellation of the construction bureaus of various counties in this province was originally intended to concentrate the functions of the county government and improve administrative efficiency. If municipal engineering were handed over to the district office for handling, separating it from the jurisdiction of the county government, it would be inconsistent with the administrative system, and would cause disputes over authority and make it difficult for affairs to proceed. Yesterday, it instructed the county government of this county that the district office's request should not be discussed, and also instructed citizens Cao Quan and others to be informed.

Shop Donations to Support Defense Expenses

The Wuxi County Defense Corps' expenses were previously discussed and decided to raise funds from four items: gentry, wealthy businessmen, shops, ships and boats, and local special products. The collection standard for shop donations is to add one-tenth to the original house donation, which has already been sent by the county to the City Fund Production Committee, which forwarded it to the Chamber of Commerce to solicit opinions. The Chamber of Commerce, believing that the listed shops, ships, and special products were all related to commerce, immediately convened a meeting and all agreed that commerce was declining and the city's donations were extremely heavy, and it was impossible to bear the additional donations for the Defense Corps. They replied requesting consideration of the merchants' difficulties and exemption from the levy. The City Fund Production Committee also believed that house donations were related to police salaries and that the recent collection numbers were short, indicating that the people's strength was declining. If repeated levies were made, it was feared that it would have an impact and it was also replied to the county requesting exemption. However, the county government believed that this shop donation had already been included in the Defense Corps' budget and approved by the provincial government and could not be left unresolved. It has decided to implement the collection from July 1 and has sent a letter to the City Fund Production Committee to handle it as scheduled. The County Chamber of Commerce, believing that this matter involved increasing the burden on merchants, brought it up for discussion at yesterday's executive supervisory meeting and decided to convene a meeting of the property owners of each section on the 25th of this month to persuade them.

Changshu

Murder Case in Haicheng

Xu Xiang's son, named Rendao, who lived in Hupu in this county and was a native of another province, was quite fierce and made a living by selling smuggled salt. In the first month of this spring, Xu transported a load of smuggled salt from Nantong to Changshu for sale. The matter was known by the local ruffians Dabai Sannv and Lu Xiaoliu, who went to report it to the anti-smuggling team stationed in the town and seized all the smuggled salt sold by Xu. Xu Rendao fled upon hearing the news. Subsequently, Lu and Dabai each received more than ten yuan in rewards. Recently, Xu learned that the smuggled salt that was seized had been reported by Lu and others, and he held a grudge and planned revenge for a long time. On the night of the 13th of this month, Xu Rendao gathered six or seven accomplices, ripped open Dabai Sannv's chest and abdomen, dug out his internal organs, and threw his body into the river. Lu Xiaoliu was beaten and bruised and fled. The next morning, Lu Xiaoliu was discovered by someone lying on the beach. When touched, he woke up and described in detail what happened last night. Nearby, there were still bloodstains, which was the place where Bai Sannv died. Lu went to the hospital for treatment and asked to apprehend the murderer.

Yang Weihang Kidnapped in Shanghai

Yang Weihang, a wealthy merchant who lives on Xueqian Street in Changshu, is about 30 years old and owns assets of 600,000 to 700,000 yuan. He opened Jintai Money Shop and Qiantaiheng Silk and Satin Bureau and other shops in Changshu. At the end of last month, he went to Shanghai for business and stayed at the Huizhong Hotel on Sanma Road (Yang is also one of the shareholders of the hotel). Unexpectedly, not long after staying there, he was kidnapped. The news was silent. The hotel telegraphed his family because a guest had suddenly disappeared, but he had not returned home. Only one accountant was left in his family. After hearing the news, he knew there had been an accident. The other day, he received another letter saying that he had been kidnapped and was now in Taihu Lake, demanding 100,000 yuan for ransom, and asking him to go to Shanghai to negotiate. Now his accountant has arrived in Shanghai to find ways to negotiate a rescue.

Zhenjiang

Boundary Demarcation Between Nanjing City and Jiangning County

The demarcation of the boundary between Jiangning County, Jiangsu Province, and Nanjing City has been brewing for three years. The principles have been stipulated by the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Interior, but the demarcation line has not yet been realized, and disputes have arisen repeatedly. Now that Jiangning County is about to move its seat, the newly appointed County Chief of Autonomy Experiment Mei Siping believes that if the boundary between the province and the city is not clearly divided, it will be difficult in administration. He has now consulted with Nanjing Mayor Shi Ying several times. Regarding the boundary issue, the county and city will directly negotiate and submit it to the provincial government for approval in the near future.

Yangzhou

Male Corpse Discovered on the Dong River Bank

An unidentified male corpse was discovered on the bank of the Dong River in Nanbaozhen, outside the South Gate of this city, this morning. He was about 20 years old, wearing a gray cloth jacket, a blue-gray undershirt, a green woolen sweater, and black cloth pants, looking like a businessman. After being discovered by the town police there, the corpse was retrieved. A total of 170 yuan in banknotes, 1 yuan in silver dollars, 780 copper coins, and a receipt from a Shanghai dental company with the words "Ms. Guo" on it were found on his body. The corpse retrieval and burial association then reported the information to the Jiangdu Court Procuratorate, which sent personnel to inspect the corpse, take photos, and post notices to claim it.

Nantong

Bloody Incident at Dasheng Factory During Labor Strike

At the Dasheng Yarn Factory in Tangzha, Nantong, over a thousand workers were laid off. On the 14th, the workers petitioned in the city to return to the factory. At 6:00 PM in the evening, they suddenly clashed with the provincial security regiment stationed at the factory. The workers wanted to rush into the Dasheng Factory, and the regiment soldiers fired warning shots, and stray bullets injured seven people. A female worker, Gu Wang, died immediately. On the 15th, party, government, military, and police held an emergency meeting in the county government. In addition to discussing and deciding on security measures for the problem of public security, representatives went to Tangzha that evening to properly negotiate with the factory about the aftermath.

Sea Guerrilla Force Reorganized

The Jiangsu Provincial Sea Guerrilla Force, which was originally stationed in the areas of Haimen and Shengshan in Nantong, has now been reorganized by the Provincial Security Department. Xu Zaiyu has been appointed as the commander-in-chief, Shen Fengshan as the commander of the first brigade, and Min Shousong as the commander of the second brigade. The coastal area of Jiangsu has been designated as the patrol area for the force, which is responsible for guerrilla warfare and pacifying the sea at any time. The headquarters is located in Yancheng. Xu Zaiyu came to Nantong from the province on the 15th to inspect his troops.

Rugao

Woman Commits Suicide After Losing Love

In the Chemahu District of this county, there is Wu Ziyan, who runs a tobacco lamp shop. He married Zhou, who has been having an affair with a neighboring Wu for many years, as if they were husband and wife. Ziyan is weak and does not interfere. Even when Wu comes, the three of them eat and sleep together, and the scandalous reputation spreads. The other day, Zhou suddenly had a quarrel with her lover, and Wu left in a rage. Wu's wife regretted it, and sadness arose from it, and she had the idea of being tired of the world. She took advantage of the fact that people were not paying attention and secretly swallowed morphine to commit suicide. Fortunately, she was noticed by a customer, Zhu, who immediately gave her treatment, so there is no worry about her life.

Elderly Woman of Seventy Met with Gruesome Assassination

In the Fengjiadai area of Rugao's Lugang District, there was an old woman surnamed Wang, over seventy years old, who had a daughter married to Zhang Zijin of Yangzhuang. When Old Man Wang passed away, he adopted his nephew Wang Fuer as his heir. They had been living together for years in relative peace. On the 10th of this month, Fuer went to Yezhuyuan for business and did not return that day. Unexpectedly, that night his adoptive mother was assassinated and died. Her eyeballs and tongue were missing, and the state was very tragic. Wang Fuer, after weeping bitterly, first put her in a coffin and then tried to find out the truth, so as to prepare to appeal to the county for redress.

Bullock Goes Berserk, Shepherd Dies

The grandson of Zhu Yu, a resident of Chemahu, who was just a child, was grazing on the 9th of this month. Unexpectedly, the bull went berserk, jumping and running wildly. Zhu was caught off guard and quickly tied the bull rope tightly around his waist. But at this time the bull had lost its docility and still ran wildly with all its might. Zhu was dragged and pulled around until someone noticed and the child had died a tragic death.

Ni Kechang and others were found to have no evidence of inciting murder and were acquitted.

Not long after, they saw four people driving in a car. The team shouted to stop the car, but they ignored it. They raised their guns and aimed, and then started the car slowly. Local News

Consular Body Discussed Factory Inspection Problem Yesterday

Meeting Secret, It Is Rumored That A Proper Solution Has Been Reached

Municipal Government's Attitude Is Based On The Principle Of Not Impairing Sovereignty

Regarding the Special General Meeting of Western Taxpayers in the Public Concession, which attempted to seize our right to inspect factories by amending the bylaws of the Yangjingbang Regulations, which has been approved by the consular body of this port and submitted to the diplomatic corps for review, the consular body of this port convened a general meeting at the American Consulate on Jiangxi Road at 2:30 PM yesterday to discuss the matter. The following is a record of the meeting.

Consuls in Attendance

Those who attended the meeting yesterday included American Consul General and Leading Consul Cunninghame, Consular Body Secretary Lange, Japanese Consul General Ishii Shotaro, French Consul General Meyrier, and more than ten consuls and representatives of various countries stationed in Shanghai.

Meeting Secret

The consuls and representatives of various countries stationed in Shanghai gathered at the American Consulate at 2:00 PM yesterday and met on the second floor of the consulate at 2:30 PM, dispersing at 3:15 PM. The content of the meeting was very secret and no press release was issued. The consuls who participated in the meeting did not easily reveal a word. Consular Body Leading Consul Cunninghame and Secretary Lange also did not say a word to the reporters who visited. However, according to reporters, after a meeting of three quarters of an hour, a concrete solution was reached.

Proper Solution

According to reliable sources, regarding the amendment to Article 34 of the bylaws of the Yangjingbang Regulations, after being approved by the consular body of this port, it was submitted to the diplomatic corps for review but was not approved. The consular body was instructed to discuss a proper solution that would take into account China's overall sovereignty on the one hand and the safety of factories in the concession on the other. The consular body convened a meeting yesterday to discuss this proper solution and has reached a decision. According to another source, the Municipal Council had previously drafted a compromise solution whereby the Municipal Council would establish a factory inspection office, and the inspectors would be Chinese hired by the Municipal Council who had received considerable factory inspection training, and a deadline would be set. This was discussed at the consular body meeting yesterday.

Municipal Government Attitude

The Municipal Government's attitude toward the inspection of factories in the concession has not changed. The sovereignty of our country's overall labor administration will not be allowed to be undermined by others. However, under the principle of not violating the central government's principles, the Municipal Government is very willing to discuss openly with the concession authorities in order to produce a proper solution. According to Secretary-General Yu, the central government has long decided on the principles of negotiation, but the Municipal Government has not had any contact with the concession authorities.

Ministry of Industry News

A Nanjing telegram on the 16th, Ministry of Industry news: Regarding the dispute over the right to inspect factories in the Shanghai concession, our side has put forward six principles. Secretary-General Yu Hongjun of the Shanghai Municipal Government and Fei Xindun, Director-General of the Municipal Council, had an informal talk last week, and the opinions were quite harmonious, but no concrete solution has been formally decided. Another informal talk is needed to exchange views. Afterwards, the two sides will discuss the cooperation methods and inspection procedures in writing. After the two sides have the same opinions, a formal meeting will be held. At that time, the Ministry of Industry will also send personnel to attend and decide on an appropriate solution.

People from Tianjin and Beiping Flee South to Seek Refuge

Passenger Volume on Northern Ocean Liners Increases Sharply

Hotel Business in Shanghai Flourishes

With the Japanese invaders approaching, Tianjin and Beiping are in danger. Wealthy people generally want to move to a better place. Therefore, recently, when liners from Tianjin arrive at the port, loading gentry from Beiping and Tianjin who come to Shanghai to seek refuge, they are filled to the brim. In the past few days, ships such as Jardine Matheson's Dingsheng, Taikoo's Niuzhuang, Tongzhou, Shuntian, and China Merchants' Yushun, when arriving in Shanghai from Tianjin, have had more than double the number of passengers compared to usual. There is almost no space on the ships. These people are all staying in hotels, so the business of major hotels is booming.

Central Mint's Coin Production Increases Daily

Reaches a New Record of 200,000 Yuan

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited the Central Mint yesterday morning and asked Li Section Chief of the secretariat about the coin production situation and the establishment of the review committee. He was informed as follows.

New Coin Production Increases Sharply

According to Li, the output of new coins in the factory has increased because the workers are all newly hired and everything must be trained from scratch. The statistics show that the output can increase by more than 10,000 yuan per day, and the progress in the past month has been particularly rapid. By last Saturday, the number of coins minted had reached 200,000 yuan per day, the highest record since the start of minting. In the future, the daily output can reach 310,000 yuan.

Review Committee Established

The fineness of silver coins is now washed and sorted by scientific methods, completely using machine power, which is already more accurate than washing and sorting by manual labor. However, for the sake of prudence, a new coin review committee has been specially formed to monitor it at any time. The list of these committee members has now been fully published. The internal regulations and organization are currently being actively prepared by the committee members. The date of establishment has not yet been determined. The newly appointed American chief technician, Grande, has now departed from the United States and will be able to take office in Shanghai at the end of this month, so the date of establishment will be determined after the chief technician arrives in Shanghai. As for the new model, it will also be brought from the United States by the chief technician.

To Be Used as Central Reserve

As for the total number of coins produced by the factory since the start of minting, the total number before and after has reached about 1.7 million yuan. It has been decided that these new coins will be used as the central bank's reserve. At the same time, because some people think that the model currently being minted is unsatisfactory, it will not be circulated on the market for the time being. Therefore, it must wait until the new model arrives before the new coins can be put into general use on the market when they are re-minted. The rumors that the review committee will review it and then circulate it on the market are speculation.

Matters Concerning Tianjin and Hangzhou Branch Factories

The head factory has no definite news about the restoration of the Tianjin and Hangzhou branch mints. However, it is found that the idea of restoring the branch factories was still at the beginning of the abolition of taels and the conversion to yuan. The intention at the time was to fear that the demand for silver coins would inevitably increase sharply after the implementation of the yuan, so it was feared that the output of the head factory would not be enough, or that the supply would not meet the demand. Therefore, it was proposed to restore the Tianjin and Hangzhou branch factories when the supply was insufficient. Now the output of coins from the head factory is increasing rapidly, so whether or not to restore them is still undecided.

Overseas Chinese General Association Formulates Measures to Assist Returned Refugee Overseas Chinese from Mexico

Re-telegraphing President Sun to Plead for Donations to Help with Emergency Relief and Sending a Letter to the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong Asking for Assistance

This time, with the persecution of Chinese in Mexico, the 40,000 overseas Chinese in Mexico have been greatly oppressed. The Global Overseas Chinese General Association in this port, in the spirit of mutual assistance, has launched a relief effort. Mayor Wu, as the local official and honorary chairman of the Overseas Chinese General Association, has vigorously promoted it and has sent letters to various agencies in the name of the mayor, urging them to provide relief. His enthusiasm is deeply appreciated. Now, in order to provide thorough relief, the Overseas Chinese General Association, in addition to giving each refugee who passes through Shanghai a relief payment of ten yuan, still feels it is not enough. It plans to raise funds in Hong Kong to accommodate the refugees and has sent a letter to the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong asking them to handle it nearby, and asking the Guangzhao Public Hall to allocate a large sum of money to help with the relief. It has also re-telegraphed President Sun to ask for relief.

Cable to President Sun

To Honorable President Sun of the Nanjing Legislative Yuan: Your cabled messages were received, but no reply has been forthcoming, which causes great concern. The distressed overseas Chinese await rescue and require funds for sustenance. We are compelled to cable again, earnestly requesting donations for immediate relief to alleviate the plight of the overseas Chinese. Can this be accommodated? We still hope for a reply. Respectfully, Huang Zhulin and others, Representatives of Distressed Overseas Chinese in Mexico. [Stamped: Xian]

Allocation of Funds for Relief

Yesterday, the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce specially dispatched its Secretary-General, Peng Canguang, together with representatives of the distressed overseas Chinese, Huang Zhulin and Lin Wenli, to the Guang Zhao Association to personally discuss the matter with its Chairman, Wen Zongyao. Mr. Wen personally received and accommodated their request. After consultation, it was unanimously agreed that the distressed overseas Chinese from Mexico, most of whom were from Guangdong, should be returned to Hong Kong and that efforts should be made to accommodate them and provide funds for their repatriation, in order to fulfill humanitarian obligations and assist fellow villagers. Mr. Wen expressed his extreme agreement and immediately promised that the Guang Zhao Association would, in conjunction with the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong, allocate substantial funds for relief. He also sent a separate letter requesting the hospital to handle the matter. It can be said that the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce's handling of the relief of distressed overseas Chinese has been thorough and comprehensive.

Letter to Hong Kong for Assistance

The original letter from the association to the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong (attached with a draft plan for relief) is excerpted below: "Regarding the matter that our 40,000 overseas Chinese compatriots in Mexico have suffered unwarranted oppression from the anti-Chinese party in Mexico. Their properties have been confiscated, they have been illegally detained, and even forcibly deported. As a result, they have fled back to the country in a state of disarray, alone and destitute, with no food or clothing, empty pockets, and no homes to return to. The cries of women and children are unbearable. Currently, more than 4,000 people have been forcibly repatriated, and another 20,000 are yet to come. If no measures are taken to support them, how can we face the distressed overseas Chinese and properly care for them? Our association, as a service organization for overseas Chinese, cannot stand idly by in the face of this situation. In addition to requesting the government to lodge a serious protest with Mexico and to quickly devise appropriate measures, the immediate need is to raise funds for relief. We have received donations of 1,000 yuan from Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and 1,000 yuan each from Shi Dezhi and Du Yuesheng, as well as the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company. Donations have also been received from the Sincere Company, China National Tobacco Corporation, Guangdong Bank, and others. However, this is merely a drop in the bucket and still insufficient. Moreover, as the distressed overseas Chinese are mostly from Guangdong, we are compelled to ask the Guang Zhao Association to allocate substantial funds so that they can be accommodated in Hong Kong and repatriated to Guangdong. The Guang Zhao Association, mindful of their fellow villagers, has readily agreed and intends to invite the Tung Wah Hospital to assist in the handling of the matter in order to achieve a concerted effort. We have long admired your hospital's dedication to charity and generosity in helping the needy. You will surely sympathize with this cause. In addition to coordinating with the Guang Zhao Association and sending separate letters to our association's representatives in Hong Kong, Chen Dasan and Lin Zishi, we dare to send this letter earnestly requesting your assistance in saving the distressed overseas Chinese and comforting our fellow villagers. The greatness of this meritorious act is no less than bringing the dead back to life. The details of the relief plan are provided in a separate document. We hope you will investigate and handle the matter and reply accordingly. Respectfully addressed to the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong. From the Presidium of the Global Chinese General Chamber of Commerce: Guo Shun, Wu Chengyu, Wang Zhengting, Zheng Hongnian, Jian Yingfu. May 26th."

Relief Measures

Draft Relief Measures for Distressed Overseas Chinese from Mexico: (1) When distressed overseas Chinese who have been deported from Mexico arrive in Shanghai, the Global Chinese General Chamber of Commerce will send personnel to receive them and provide each person with a small amount of pocket money for sustenance. (2) When the aforementioned distressed overseas Chinese arrive in Hong Kong, the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong will assign responsible personnel to receive them upon arrival, provide accommodation and food, and purchase boat tickets to assist them in returning to their hometowns. (3) All relief expenses required in Hong Kong will be jointly borne by the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong and the Guang Zhao Association in Shanghai, or efforts will be made to raise sufficient funds. (4) For each batch of distressed overseas Chinese returning to Hong Kong, the Global Chinese General Chamber of Commerce will provide a list of names and the ship's schedule and name to the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong for verification and reception. (5) In order to prevent problems and facilitate relief, the Global Chinese General Chamber of Commerce will issue certificates of identification to the distressed overseas Chinese (one per person) for verification and to prevent abuse. The format will be determined separately. Respectfully submitted by the Global Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai.

Yesterday, Citizens' Associations of Two Special Districts Inspected Goods of Enemy Origin

Secret Informant Box Established

Announcement Issued

The First Special District Citizens' United Association, in order to eliminate goods of enemy origin within the district, first inspected stores along Henan Road the day before yesterday. As the task was not completed, it continued yesterday. Shen Yuntao, Tong Shuangyang, Zhu Zhichun, Fang Peicheng, Ge Futian, Chen Shude, and others inspected more than 100 establishments, including the Civilization Printing House and the Commercial Press, and found no goods of enemy origin. In order to alert unscrupulous merchants, the association has established a secret informant box at its headquarters since yesterday, soliciting confidential reports. Yesterday, someone confidentially reported that a large quantity of goods of enemy origin had entered the cotton yarn and iron industries on Suzhou Road. The association plans to send personnel to investigate immediately, to ensure that goods of enemy origin are eliminated and unscrupulous merchants disappear.

The National Goods Promotion Committee of the Second Special District Citizens' United Association began inspecting goods of enemy origin yesterday. Recognizing that goods of enemy origin have recently flooded the market and have been disguised by unscrupulous merchants, not only are customers easily deceived, but the future of national goods is also significantly affected. The association issued a special announcement to all national goods merchants and factories, requesting them to report their products for verification and introduction. The original text is as follows: "For public notification: It has been found that goods of enemy origin have recently flooded the market, and counterfeit national goods are particularly prevalent, leading to confusion and making it impossible to distinguish between them. Not only are customers deceived, but national goods merchants and factories are also harmed. In view of this, this association has resolved to announce that national goods merchants and factories may have their products verified and introduced by this association. At the same time, we will investigate counterfeit products to eliminate confusion. Therefore, we hereby notify all manufacturers that if you have excellent products, please send samples to the association for examination so that we can verify and introduce them. If you discover counterfeit products, please report them to the association for handling. This announcement is made." The association also announced to employees and workers of various shops yesterday: "For public notification: It has been found that some patriotic groups have used explosives to warn unscrupulous merchants, which has harmed innocent employees and workers. Therefore, we hereby notify all manufacturers, workers, and shop employees that if you discover goods of enemy origin, please report them to this association to avoid being implicated."

Citizens Propose Levying Rent

To Supplement Aviation Donations

According to the Guowen News Agency, since the fundraising for the National Aviation Salvation Fund began in this city, citizens such as Huang Ciwei, with patriotic enthusiasm, have petitioned the municipal government to levy one or two months' rent to supplement the aviation donations. If their rent is levied to support aviation, it would not only be a fair measure but also greatly please the public. It is reported that many people support this proposal, and the municipal government is currently evaluating and processing it.

Many People Saw Him Off Yesterday

Mr. Grahame, the British Assessor in China, retired due to old age and set off to return home yesterday on the British India Steam Navigation Company's ship "Carthage." He has been in Shanghai for 12 years and is known for his integrity and his enthusiasm for social welfare. Therefore, many people saw him off yesterday, and everyone was reluctant to part with him.

Shanghai Municipal Council Clarifies That the Police Department Does Not Use Torture

On the 2nd of this month, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, based on a report from the Shanghai United Association of Patriotic Organizations, stated that Luo Sizhang and Lu Yong were subjected to cruel treatment when they were captured by the Public Concession police in December of last year. They sent a letter to the Municipal Council requesting clarification. The Deputy Secretary-General of the Municipal Council has now replied to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, stating that your association also believes that this is unlikely to be true. The truth is that Luo Sizhang and Lu Yong were captured on December 22nd of last year in Room 41 of the Unity Hotel at 344 North Hai Road. The workers were members of the so-called Blood Soul Assassination Group, and they were accused of being affiliated with bandits and illegally possessing explosives. They were subsequently sentenced to three months imprisonment each by the court. As for the allegation that the police used torture, it has been found to be completely untrue. Neither of the defendants complained of mistreatment, either at the police station or in court. During the first interrogation, Luo Sizhang requested medical treatment, which was immediately granted after examination. It was found that he had a carbuncle that had just been surgically removed, and the bandage was still in place.

U.S. Marine Corps Commander Colonel Gilder Died of Illness Yesterday Morning

According to the Greater America Evening Post, Colonel Gilder, Commander of the 4th Regiment of the U.S. Marine Corps stationed in Shanghai, died of illness at Hong'en Hospital at 0:50 AM this morning (the 16th), at the age of only 51. Colonel Gilder was the most popular officer in the U.S. Marine Corps stationed in Shanghai and was loved by both his superiors and subordinates. He was assigned to Shanghai after the previous Commander, Colonel Holcomb, was discharged due to heart disease and took office in March. However, a week ago, he was hospitalized due to overwork and nervous exhaustion. It was expected that he would recover after a few weeks of rest, but unexpectedly, he suddenly suffered from hemorrhage last night and died despite all efforts. The sad news has shocked the country. The flag was lowered to half-mast this morning, and the soldiers wore mourning bands to express their grief. His wife in Shanghai is in great sorrow and has fainted. His mother is still in New York and is expected to be deeply grieved upon hearing the news. Colonel Gilder's remains have been moved to the American Funeral Parlor. The date of the funeral has not yet been determined. It is reported that Colonel Gilder is the fourth commander of the 4th Regiment of the U.S. Marine Corps to die suddenly. Since Colonel Hill led the entire regiment to Shanghai in 1927, he committed suicide with a gun the following year. His successor, Colonel Davis, died of a sudden heart attack a few weeks after leaving office. His successor, Colonel Lemmon, is still alive. In recent years, only one commander of the regiment has remained alive after completing his term of service in Shanghai. Moreover, Colonel Holcomb died suddenly of heart disease on Christmas Eve last year, and Colonel Gilder died of cerebral hemorrhage just two months after taking office. The vacant position will be temporarily filled by Lieutenant Colonel Morse, who previously served as acting commander.

Shanghai Municipal Council Sends Condolences for the Death of the U.S. Military Commander

Colonel Gilder, Commander of the 4th Regiment of the U.S. Marine Corps stationed in Shanghai, passed away yesterday morning. Mr. Bell, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, immediately sent a letter to Mr. Morse, Deputy Commander of the regiment, expressing his deep regret. He stated that it was regrettable that Colonel Gilder had died shortly after returning to Shanghai and taking office, following the death of his predecessor, Colonel Holcomb. He expressed his condolences to the 4th Regiment and Colonel Gilder's family.

U.S. Fleet Sailed to Northern China Yesterday Morning

The U.S. fleet, which arrived in Shanghai at the end of last month, including 13 destroyers, submarines No. 37, No. 39, and No. 41, the aircraft carrier "Canopus," and the transport ships "Huntress" and "Black Hawk," except for the "Huntress," which left Shanghai for Qin Island on the 9th of this month, the remaining ships also weighed anchor and sailed to Yantai and Qingdao in northern China yesterday morning at around 5 AM.

Mail to Luandong Delivered as Usual

Postal Rates to Nanyang Are Adjusted According to Gold Prices, Not Increased

Regarding postal matters, a reporter from the Central News Agency learned the following from responsible officials of the Directorate General of Posts: (1) Revised postal rates for letters sent from private postal agencies to Nanyang. The postal rates for international mail have always been calculated based on the gold franc exchange rate. Since the price of gold has risen, the postal rates for letters sent from our country to foreign countries have gradually increased from 10 cents to 25 cents. The same applies to letters sent to Nanyang. However, in order to show consideration for overseas Chinese, the postal rate for letters sent from private postal agencies to Nanyang is still only 5 cents (half of the previous international postal rate) and has not been uniformly changed. Recently, due to the extremely difficult financial situation of the postal service, the postal administration has incurred excessive losses in paying the shipping costs for these items in gold francs. It was forced to revise the rates according to the gold franc exchange rate, but still maintain the principle of half-price, charging only 12.5 cents in national currency to show preferential treatment. As for letters from private postal agencies sent from Nanyang, the local postal administration has already increased the rate from one-half to two-thirds of the international postal rate, which is higher than the postage collected in our country. This adjustment is actually based on gold prices and is not an increase in charges. This postage increase was originally scheduled to take effect on May 1st, but it was temporarily postponed because the overseas Chinese were not fully aware of the situation. The Ministry of Communications is now consulting with the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to provide a proper explanation, and it should be implemented soon. (2) Mail to and from all bureaus in Luandong is being handled as usual. Although the military situation in North China is very tense, all post offices in Luandong are still operating as usual, and mail to and from the area can be sent through. The report that mail to Qinhuangdao and Changli has been suspended is not true. The postal administration has not issued such a notice.

International Trade Bureau to Establish Research Committee

To Guide the Overseas Development of National Products

According to the Central News Agency, an official in charge of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry stated to reporters yesterday that the dumping of foreign goods has greatly affected national industries. Therefore, the Trade Bureau is paying attention to the dumping of foreign goods and reporting them to the Ministry of Industry at any time in order to find countermeasures. It is also studying the current situation of national goods trade and guiding its improvement. His remarks are summarized below:

Responding to Dumping

According to the statement, foreign goods have recently adopted a policy of planned price reductions and dumping against our country. For example, according to a letter from a friend, a certain foreign industrial and commercial consortium, united under the leadership of its government, is engaged in malicious commercial competition against our country. Its purpose is to bankrupt our country's industry and commerce in order to achieve its ambition of economic aggression. The government, in view of this, has established a dumping tax committee to collect dumping taxes and protect national infant industries. The Ministry of Industry, whose responsibility it is to guide and protect national industries, is considering countermeasures to remedy the situation. Therefore, the Trade Bureau is paying close attention to this and will report its findings to the Ministry of Industry for study at any time.

Guidance to Industry and Commerce

For the above reasons, the Trade Bureau will strengthen its ties with national goods factories and various national goods movements in the future in order to gain a thorough understanding of the current state of national industry and provide guidance. At 1 PM this afternoon, the National Goods Movement Committee of the First Special District Citizens' United Association will hold the Second National Goods Movement Promotion Meeting at the Ningbo Native Place Association. The Trade Bureau has assigned Li Zejin and Chen Jingsheng of the Guidance Section to attend and participate. In the future, if there are similar gatherings, the Bureau will also send personnel to attend and provide guidance.

Sino-Russian Trade

After the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, all trade relations will be gradually restored. The Ministry of Industry believes that Russian trade is mainly conducted by the government. Therefore, it has decided to establish a Trade Bureau to handle trade with Russia in order to coordinate everything. The regulations for the bureau's organization are currently being drafted by the Ministry. However, whether it will be subordinate to the International Trade Bureau or directly subordinate to the Ministry of Industry is still under consideration and will be decided after Director He recovers from his illness and is discharged from the hospital, and after consultation with Minister Chen Gongbo.

Trade Research

The Trade Bureau will establish an International Trade Research Committee to study the trade policies and current situation of various countries in order to discuss the attitude that our country should take towards international trade and to guide and assist the overseas development of national industries. The regulations for the committee's organization are still under review. Preparations will begin as soon as they are approved by the Ministry. As for the members of the committee, domestic economic experts and industry giants will be appointed.

Ministry of Railways Allocates Emergency Relief Funds to Shaanxi

Totaling 62,500 Yuan

Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, has been receiving telegrams from the Shaanxi Provincial Government for several days, which state that since May 1st, the weather in the Weibei area of Shaanxi Province has suddenly changed. On the 2nd and 3rd, strong winds arose, destroying roofs and uprooting trees and crops. This was followed by heavy frost and heavy snow, causing great damage. Furthermore, there has been no rain after the frost and snow. If rain does not continue to fall, there is no hope of recovery, and the livelihood of dozens of counties will be cut off. Upon receiving the telegrams, Yu Youren believed that the disaster in Shaanxi was extremely serious. In addition to remitting 62,500 yuan of emergency relief funds allocated by the Ministry of Railways to the Shaanxi Relief Committee for relief yesterday, he is now trying to appeal to all parties for assistance. As for the Feng University students, except for a small number of volunteers who are still fighting on the front lines, the rest remain in Beiping. Feng University has nothing except the campus and its teachers and students. If war breaks out in the old capital, Feng University is determined to coexist with the old capital.
