The Rapid Progress of the Wusong Merchant Marine School of the Ministry of Communications

▲Excellent Students Have Great Career Prospects

▲Opening High School and Enrolling Vocational Students

The Merchant Marine School is a specialized school directly under the Ministry of Communications, with the purpose of training maritime talents. It was founded in the late Qing Dynasty and discontinued for more than ten years after the early Republic. In the 18th year of the Republic, the Ministry of Communications, in view of the need for maritime personnel, reopened it. It is divided into (Navigation Department) and (Mechanical Engineering Department), both of which graduate in four years (two years of schoolwork and two years of internship). After graduation, the Ministry issues corresponding seafarer certificates, which allow them to serve as seafarers of corresponding ranks on ocean-going and coastal ships (such as second mate, chief mate, ship master, second engineer, chief engineer, and chief engineer).

▲The positions of the graduates are as follows: The graduates of the early Republic are now serving as shipowners, chief shipowners, pilots, etc. Their reputation and achievements are recognized by the Chinese people. For example, the current chief shipowner of Zhaoxing Company, Mr. Chen Ganqing, the chief shipowner of Ning Shao Company, Mr. Shen Jiyun, the director of the Jianghai Customs Pilotage Bureau, Mr. Lin Guojie, the director of the China Merchants Bureau, Mr. Yang Zhixiong, and the current principal of the school, Mr. Xu Zufan, all graduated from the school in the early Republic. The school's admission requirements and treatment are described below:

▲Admission Qualifications: Graduates of accredited high schools or equivalent schools may apply for the first year during the recruitment period.

▲Tuition, Room and Board, and Miscellaneous Fees: No tuition, room and board, or any miscellaneous fees such as lecture notes and sports are charged. Students pay 25 yuan per semester for meals (the school subsidizes an additional 10 yuan). Students in the Navigation Department who are assigned to various ships for internships and students in the Mechanical Engineering Department who are assigned to factories for internships have separate regulations for meal and accommodation subsidies. Uniform and book fees are approximately several tens of yuan per academic year. The first class of students in the Navigation Department are currently assigned to various bureaus and company ships such as China Merchants, Ning Shao, Zhaoxing, Zhengji, and Sanbei for internships. Some have already taken on the duties of seafarers.

▲The Graduates of This Session Already Have a Future: The aforementioned first class of students will formally graduate in the summer of this year, and most have already obtained seafarer positions. The second class of students in the Navigation Department are currently interning on the China Merchants Bureau's Fairness ship. Since this spring, Principal Xu and the China Merchants authorities have consulted and agreed, and the Ministry of Communications has approved the designation of the Fairness ship to accommodate the school's students for internships. The above are the past and present situations of the school.

▲Opening an Affiliated High School: It is also heard that the school's original preparatory course has been abolished. Now, in order to broaden training and facilitate sequential promotion to higher education, the Ministry of Communications has approved the addition of an affiliated high school, which will enroll students and open classes in the summer of this year. At the same time, the Navigation Department and the Mechanical Engineering Department must also recruit new students.

Shanghai Law College Recovers School Buildings

丨All School Buildings Destroyed in the January 28th Incident丨

丨Will Soon Be Fully Restored丨

▲Decided to Restore the Library Collection at the Same Time

▲Moving Back to Jiangwan Road Office at the End of June

The Shanghai Law College (formerly known as the Law University) on Jiangwan Road in Zhabei was founded by Chu Fucheng and Shen Junru. Originally without a single tile or beam, they rented houses for lectures. Over the years, the two men worked hard to build school buildings on the rented land. In the spring of the 19th year, the classrooms and student dormitories were completed at the same time. The classrooms could accommodate more than 1,650 people, and the dormitories could accommodate more than 600 people. The remaining dormitories were temporarily rented. In the winter of that year, the Ministry of Education sent personnel to investigate and recognized the excellent results, and specially approved the registration to encourage them. In the autumn of the previous year, a large auditorium was added, with a magnificent and resplendent architecture, also capable of accommodating more than 1,650 people. It was also planned to continue building a library and student dormitory in the spring of the next year, because the school had more than 1,040 students at the time, and the dormitories were deeply inadequate. Unexpectedly, not long after the completion of the auditorium, the original aspiration was not fulfilled, and the January 28th Incident suddenly broke out. Three days later, the Japanese army used machine guns and flamethrowers to burn it, causing the school, built with years of effort, to be completely destroyed in two days and nights, with a loss of more than 400,000 yuan. Despite the pain, the two men still worked hard to maintain it and did not lose heart because of it. It is now learned that the school is more actively handling the matter and has decided to rebuild the school buildings. A contract has been signed with the Meichang Construction Company at the end of last month to start construction immediately and rebuild on the original site. All classrooms, auditoriums, dormitories, offices, etc. have been further improved and restored to their original appearance. The construction must be completed by the end of August so that it can be used when school starts in the next semester. The required construction cost of 150,000 yuan has been arranged by the school authorities and the Restoration Committee. The school is scheduled to move back to the original site on Jiangwan Road at the end of June to take care of the progress of the project. It is heard that the school has also decided to restore all the collections of the destroyed library at the same time, and is currently making every effort to solicit and collect them, and plans to allocate funds to build a large-scale independent library building in the shortest possible time.

Chaoyang College of Peiping to Establish a Branch in Shanghai This Summer

It is recently learned that Chaoyang College of Peiping is preparing to establish a branch in Shanghai. This college is formerly Chaoyang University of Beijing, a renowned law school in the old capital, founded in the second year of the Republic by Wang Youling, Jiang Yong, and others. The current president is Jiang Yong, and the chairman of the board is Huang Fu. The college emphasizes practicality and has been earnest in its management and perfect in its operations for twenty years. It has repeatedly received awards and commendations from the former Ministries of Education and Law, as well as the current Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Judicial Administration. Its graduates have achieved outstanding results, especially in the judicial examinations. Since the establishment of the Republic, only seven formal examinations have been held, and graduates of this school have won the first place six times. They have also repeatedly obtained top marks in the civil service or county magistrate examinations in Beijing, Peiping, and Shandong. At the Hague Conference in the eighteenth year, the French jurist Escarra specifically cited this school as the best law school in China in his report to the international community. It is heard that the school still has more than 2,000 students. Recently, due to the invasion of the Japanese bandits, approaching northern Hebei, in order to facilitate the students who are eager to enroll in the college this summer, it has been decided to establish a branch in Shanghai this summer. The location has been found on Yaozhu Jiao Road, and arrangements have been finalized. A preparatory office has been set up in Liu's residence at No. 1 Yilu, Ying'er Dong Road, in the French Concession, and all preparations are actively underway. New students will soon be recruited in this city on a scheduled basis.

Chen Guofu Resigns from the Board of Directors of China Public School

Central Committee member Chen Guofu was once elected as a director of the China Public School. The Customs Specialization School's Foreign Affairs Class Will Enroll Students

The Second Branch of the Customs Specialization School is located in Shanghai, specializing in cultivating talents for foreign affairs within customs. Since the customs tariff autonomy, the tax regulations have been revised, and the rates are now higher than before. Some people with a greedy desire for profit have been evading taxes and smuggling. Therefore, the customs needs more personnel for foreign affairs. Graduates of the school in previous years have all been assigned to various customs offices. It is recently learned that the school, in order to train advanced foreign affairs talents, has increased the difficulty of the coursework and changed the graduation period to two years. This summer, it will enroll 60 new students.

Due to German Anti-Semitism, the Next Olympics May Not Be Held in Germany

丨Opinion Expressed by the President of the US Olympic Committee丨

World Games should not be held in countries that discriminate against other races. The International Olympic Committee will discuss this at its Vienna meeting this summer.

(Baltimore, USA) Mr. Brent Tuthaker, the president of the US Olympic Committee, recently sent a letter to Mr. Miller, the editor of the Baltimore Jewish Daily, expressing his personal views on the German anti-Semitism. Burt believes that the World Olympic Games should not be held in a country that conflicts with the fundamental principle of national equality of the Olympic Games. The next World Olympic Games in 1936 has already been approved to be held in Berlin. Burt's letter states as follows:

Regarding the letter concerning Germany's ban on Jews participating in the World Games and the steps it has already taken, the reply is as follows: The direct handling and refereeing rights of the World Olympic Games are in the hands of the World Olympic Committee. The meeting will be held in Vienna this summer, and this matter will undoubtedly be raised at the conference. My personal opinion is that the World Games should not be held in a country that conflicts with the fundamental principle of national equality of the World Games. The mutual agreements of the Olympic Games are not limited by class, color, or race. The US Olympic Committee will discuss this matter first.

Special Publication

General Overview of Education in European Countries (1)

— Recorded by Lu Bingqian

丨Speech by Cheng Qibao at the Municipal Education Bureau丨

The topic I will be discussing today can be roughly divided into four parts: (1) the process of this observation, (2) the general situation of education in various countries, (3) the trends of education in Europe, and (4) the problems of education in China.

1. The Process of Observation

The time for our observation this time was very short. In actual calculation, it was only about six months. We passed through almost nine countries, spending an average of only about two weeks in each country. With such a short time, it was naturally impossible to make thorough inquiries and investigations. What we saw were just some incomplete impressions. Therefore, the expectations of the general public for us were originally very high, thinking that after this observation, we would definitely make a great contribution and be able to prescribe a remedy for China's education to cure the chronic diseases of the past twenty years. However, the fact is that we inevitably failed their expectations. This point, before I start speaking, should be explained to you first. In the future, we still hope that everyone will be guided by the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation to open up a brand new path for Chinese education.

I remember from the year before last to the first month of last year, European countries had a Chinese education observation group come to China. Among them, one was the German Minister of Education, one was a French scientist, and one was a British scientist and economist. They came to China to observe education for a very short time and traveled very little, only visiting Hangzhou, Shanghai, Tianjin, and Nanjing. Recently, they have a report that, although very detailed, they also feel that their observation situation cannot be thoroughly understood and have requested the Chinese government to send a few people to Europe to exchange actual situations with each other. At that time, the Chinese government very much approved of this proposal, so it sent five people to Europe to observe for eight months. During these eight months, the various countries they visited were very friendly to us. Whenever they went to a place, they would receive a warm reception and welcome. We feel that China's foreign friendship is not bad. They were able to express sympathy and thorough understanding for our observation this time. Therefore, our trip was not only shouldering our mission but also increased a lot of international friendship. There is also one thing that we feel very ashamed about, that is, many places in European countries do not understand the situation in China. The big places are still okay, but when they arrive in small places, they are just like us when we see foreigners, finding it very strange to see us shaking hands and talking with them. This is really due to China's lack of propaganda abroad. Japan is not like that. For example, in the Sino-Japanese problem, Japan desperately promotes itself abroad, even buying many newspapers. Many newspapers in Poland are bought by Japan. Chinese diplomacy lacks this kind of courage, so it feels a lot of difficulties. They are not unwilling to provide assistance to China, but unfortunately, they do not understand the situation in China very well. Although this issue is small, we should also pay attention to it.

2. The Educational Situation in Various Countries

Because the impressions gained from six months of observation are very complex, it is not easy to sort them out clearly. Today, I can only give a summary report. If there is a chance in the future, I will discuss them separately.

European countries have all undergone extremely great changes in education in the fifteen years after the war. They have suffered from the wounds of the war and feel the need to reform the educational system and methods. This reform can be seen from two aspects in general. On the one hand, because of the revival of modern nations, to make their own nations continue to flourish, naturally, they rely on the power of education. The past war did not know how many human lives and properties were lost. Although there are many main reasons, the error of the educational methods is also one of them. The obvious errors are roughly three points: (1) The past education was too nationalistic. The knowledge and methods of education were all focused on maintaining the survival of the state. Therefore, an uncongenial phenomenon was created between countries. Everywhere, their own country was regarded as important, and international conflicts arose. (2) The past education was too materialistic. The result of education was that everyone only sought profit, only sought material satisfaction, and did not ask about spiritual comfort, so that personal life could not be equalized, and social conflicts also arose. (3) The past education was too intellectualized, regarding schools as places for seeking knowledge and not seeking personal life adaptation. With these three points, the unprecedented European War was indirectly brewed. Now, to build a new nation, they should build their own nation on the foundation of reason and adapt culture to the needs of the nation. On the one hand, they advocate education of geniuses, hoping that everyone can use their talents to discover new creations, and then integrate them with the old culture to create a new culture. This kind of change is from a general perspective. The degree and methods of educational change in the eight countries observed this time are also different. They can be roughly divided into four categories: (1) England and France, in fact, the degree of their change is very shallow. (2) Emerging countries, after the war, based on the spirit of national self-determination, established many small countries, such as Poland and Czechoslovakia. They did not have an educational system in the past. After establishing the country, they had to start from scratch, create a new educational system, and establish a new educational system. There are many materials in the middle that can be used for our reference. (3) Germany and Austria, after the war, their political systems changed, and their educational systems and methods also changed. (4) The most noteworthy and interesting are Russia and Italy. These two countries are absolutely different in political system and seem to be unable to come together. In fact, Russia practices a communist political system, and political power is in the hands of the proletariat. Italy is also a one-party dictatorship. It regards education as a tool of politics, and the strength of education is relied upon to implement political propositions. Their situation is the same as China's and is worthy of our special attention. The following will be explained separately.

Spring and Autumn

Being Deflated

— Zhanlu

The two words "being deflated" are a kind of slang popular in Suzhou and Shanghai, the meaning of which seems to have the meaning of knocking people down; but knocking down is done with the hand, and being deflated is done with the mouth, and the effect of the mouth is even more ferocious than the effect of the hand. Therefore, people who are knocked down sometimes fall quickly, and climb up even faster; and people who are deflated, if they want to return to their original state, and be as full of muscles and plump of skin as before, then this should respond to a sentence by Mr. Dongfang: "How easy is it to talk about?"

Let me give two examples: A person who is knocked down is only beaten with a stuffy stick; if the constitution is weak and cannot withstand this major blow, then he will be depressed, and never recover again. If not, jumping up from the ground, snatching the other person's stuffy stick, "treating the other person in the way they treated you," then the person who was knocked down can also knock down the other person to vent this anger. As for the person who is deflated, then there is very little hope! The fat and flesh have been sucked away by people, leaving only the empty skin of a "flat collapsed candle," but he still wants to eat a reassuring pill, thinking that he can definitely be as full of muscles and plump of skin as before; hey! Go read a "Classic of Difficulties"! I'm afraid it's a thousand times difficult, more difficult than anything else.

China is a crystal clear and plump honey peach; if the gluttonous enemy keeps sucking it, then it is naturally in a position of being deflated. But, not all countries in the world are honey peaches that are easily deflated. Why is Germany paying very close attention to the Pacific islands, but now doesn't want to take them back? Dare to ask, is Germany being deflated by the Orientals? Why is the Soviet Union, which is unwilling to give in on the Middle East Railway, now willing to sell it to its enemies? Dare to ask, is Russia being deflated by the Orientals? Although that is the case, Germany and Russia being deflated by the Orientals still retain their faces; Germany is only half deflated, and Russia is only quasi-deflated, only our old empire, transformed into a young Republic of China, is completely deflated! Half-deflated is Deflated Big, quasi-deflated is Deflated Two, and completely deflated is actually a Deflated Three! Recently, Deflated Two sold the Middle East Railway, and our government protested to the Soviet Union; as a result, we were rebuffed, and fell into a criticism of "losing moral rights." Alas! Deflated Two is dealing with Deflated Big, of course, it doesn't dare to do anything, but now the one protesting is not Deflated Big, but Deflated Three; then, the quasi-deflated Deflated Two is going to deflate the completely deflated Deflated Three again!

According to the appetite of the Orientals, they almost want to deflate the countries of the whole world before they can be happy; but, can a dwarf's stomach really swallow such a big Earth? After swallowing it, will a volcanic eruption not occur in his belly? This is a question.

Refugee

— Yang Yusheng

Because domestic politics are not on the right track, social organizations are imperfect, and it is very difficult for the unemployed to find work. Even with work, it is difficult to maintain a living. Therefore, compatriots who sell their sweat and blood try every possible means to sneak abroad. Although all the power of life and death is in the hands of foreigners, and they have to live an inhuman life, fortunately, patience and hard work are the characteristics of the Chinese. Therefore, under their hard work, they can stand firm, and many people indeed make a fortune. They are perched above the various classes of people in the country and are called overseas Chinese.

They can use methods to get money from foreigners and can also contribute money back to the country to subsidize the funds needed for various new national salvation terms. From China's point of view, of course, this is the best thing. However, in the eyes of foreigners, they really cannot stand it. Their own country is experiencing an economic downturn, and there are many unemployed people. If they were to let the Chinese, whom they consider as despicable as dogs, steal their jobs, it would be a case of "leading beasts to eat people, how can they be parents of the people?" Therefore, the "parents" of the general foreigners, for the sake of their people, no country, whether it is a large country, a small country, a strong country, or a weak country, is not desperately driving away overseas Chinese. As for the methods of driving them away, they can be roughly divided into two types: artistic and inartistic. Japan's method of driving away overseas Chinese is burning, looting, and killing, which is the most inartistic method. The Philippines, Siam, the United States, and Mexico are much more artistic. They first use various heavy taxes to make it impossible for overseas Chinese to gain a foothold and have to leave. If they still cannot be driven away, the methods of burning, looting, and killing may be imitated. Now, the overseas Chinese in Mexico already feel that it is impossible to stay, and they are fleeing back to their motherland in batches in a very embarrassed manner. These are the "refugees" mentioned in this article, a term as novel as "disaster officials."

In fact, since we are born in this 20th century full of murderous intent, and unfortunately dispatched by God to China full of death, we can only be optimistic and live day by day. Moreover, the political instability, imperfect social organization, and the inability to settle unemployed people, which are generally worried about, are only temporary problems. As long as you take "immortality pills" to prolong your life and wait, even if you cannot get your wish in your lifetime, you must make a will, ordering your sons, grandsons, great-grandsons, great-great-grandsons,... rather wait quietly for God's will to die than presumptuously try to survive by human plans. Don't worry, there will be a day when you will see a prosperous scene. There is really no need to travel across the ocean to suffer the dirty air of foreigners. If you insist on going against the will of heaven, then no one will be responsible for all the misfortunes that come, and no one will dare to ask about it. It is truly pitiful to have suffering that cannot be spoken and grievances that cannot be expressed!

Long Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 6: Sweet and Bitter Love Field, Coldly Observing and Commenting on Two Sides, Rugged World, Secret Agreement for Three Years

Ji Zhi smiled. He raised his shoulders a couple of times and said: You are just saying that casually, without sincerity. Are you promising to come tomorrow, or are you promising to come the day after tomorrow? And... Gui Zhi said with a straight face: After all, it's just these words, what am I coming for? Ji Zhi said; I have to ask you again, why did you promise the two words? Gui Zhi couldn't help but chuckle and said: You don't need to ask, we are just making do now. Whenever you tell us to come, we will come. We dare not be late, huh? Saying that, she smiled again. Seeing this, Ji Zhi knew that he could not keep her here, so he had to put down his hand and nodded, saying: You are too kind, you are too kind. It will be at this time tomorrow that we will meet here, rain or shine. Gui Zhi said with a faint smile: Alright. Ji Zhi smiled: No, no, you are promising so casually, how would I know if you will come? Gui Zhi said: Then, how should I promise? Ji Zhi said: You have to say that's how it will be done. Gui Zhi nodded slightly and said: Oh! That's how it will be done. The last word of that sentence was dragged out extremely long. Ji Zhi said: You see, you always promise me so casually. But I know, you are joking with me, you will come tomorrow. Gui Zhi didn't say anything more to him, she pulled him away and stepped out of the door of the private room. In order to make the appointment for tomorrow more concrete, Ji Zhi followed her behind, all the way to the door. Gui Zhi turned around and said: Don't see me off, I don't want you to see me off. Ji Zhi smiled: If you don't want me to see you off, I won't, but... Gui Zhi smiled: I won't come tomorrow, you just wait. Saying that, she twisted her body and left. Ji Zhi felt that her attitude was very lively at this time, and naturally he was very happy in his heart. She said she wouldn't come tomorrow, that's exactly when she would come, he would wait for her early tomorrow. Ji Zhi thought like this, and happily walked back into the private room to clear the bill for the refreshments. Before he had even stepped into the door, he heard someone in the private room next door call out Ji Zhi. He recognized the voice immediately, it was his elder brother, Hou Zhi. This was strange, when did he come? He must have heard everything I just said to Gui Zhi. Involuntarily, his heart began to pound. While he was hesitating, the second call of Ji Zhi came out, which really made it difficult for him. However, how could he escape? He had to bite the bullet and walk to the private room next door. Cigarettes

— A Jie

The only consolation for those of us who live a monotonous life outside is "cigarettes." Liu Ling used wine as a consolation, and Lu Tong used tea as a consolation. How could they know that besides tea and wine, there are also cigarettes? Drinking too much wine can lead to insanity; drinking too much tea is also tasteless. Only this paper-rolled cigarette is a wonderful thing to relieve worries and leave behind joy. Kissing it from time to time, it is more lovely than a beautiful woman.

A beautiful woman is something to be admired but not to be trifled with, just like a flower. However, some like the rich and beautiful flowers like peonies and芍藥, while others like the pure and beautiful flowers like plums, chrysanthemums, and芙蓉; some like the gorgeous flowers like蔴蕪, red bananas, peaches, and plums; some like the淡沱 flowers like水葓, osmanthus, and morning glory. This is because everyone has different views. Only cigarettes are not for appreciation but for playing with, just like every family has a housewife, and everyone wants to embrace a yellow-faced woman. This is a phenomenon in our noble country at the moment!

When there is something to do, smoking a cigarette can refresh you; when there is nothing to do, smoking a cigarette can relieve boredom; after meals and after drinking, cigarettes are especially essential. If you, old man, have made up your mind to use your sword of wisdom to cut off the threads of love, you will always fail. Therefore, the name of cigarettes is "love grass," which shows its magic.

Cigarettes can also enhance the love between husband and wife. Occasionally, when your wife is angry, gentle consideration and sweet words cannot work. As long as you, old man, respectfully offer a cigarette, light a match, and bring it to your wife's cherry lips, naturally she will smile sweetly and a hundred charms will be born, which can fill the sea of hatred, can fill the sky of love, and you will feel unexpected effects, avoiding the skit of Chen Jichang dressing up and kneeling in the pond. According to this geometric theorem, if applied to adults and gentlemen, it will definitely have the same unexpected effect. Therefore, cigarettes can also be called "magic wands." I have never dared to admit the saying that cigarettes are harmful.

Small Recipes

Soft-Shelled Turtle and Crucian Carp

— Zui Chi Sheng

Soft-shelled turtle, also known as 鱉, is best with a blue-white abdomen, produced in inland rivers. It is a beneficial food in spring. It is most fresh when rapeseed flowers are yellow and peonies are blooming. Therefore, it is called "rapeseed flower soft-shelled turtle" and "peony soft-shelled turtle." The best way to eat it is stewed clearly. However, it must be washed and scraped clean. First, add water and boil it slightly until it boils, then remove the water and place it in a jar. Add southern ham, bamboo shoots, winter mushrooms, diced pork fat, rock sugar, Chen wine, and a little salt and ginger. Cover tightly and simmer over low heat until tender. It is very clear, fat, and delicious. If you add two or three red dates to cook together, it can remove the fishy taste. In addition, in Cantonese cuisine, soft-shelled turtle and black chicken feet are cooked together, named Phoenix Claw Water Fish, which also has a special flavor. However, it seems unsuitable to eat in summer. It is said that soft-shelled turtles are poisonous if they are sucked by mosquitoes, and are called "mosquito soft-shelled turtles." Only when "osmanthus soft-shelled turtles" are on the market in August and September can you gorge yourself. In addition, crucian carp lacks freshness in summer. According to fishermen, after the Beginning of Summer, water rats can transform into crucian carp, so it is also advisable not to eat them.

Wisteria Flower Cake

— Yi Qiu

When the wisteria flowers bloom in spring and summer in villages or courtyards (commonly known as 藤簍花 in the north), the villagers say that there are both male and female flowers. The color is purple, but the male ones are more gorgeous and have no fragrance, only for passers-by to appreciate. The female ones are light in color and fragrant, and can be used to make cakes, which are extremely delicious. When my father was alive, he loved them the most. Now, when the wisteria flowers are in full bloom, I will describe the method below for greedy comrades. Pick dozens of female flowers, remove the calyxes, and wash the petals in clean water. Use four taels of flour, two eggs, and two taels of white sugar (those who like sweets can add a little). Mix with half a bowl of clean water, then mix the washed petals into the mixture, pour it into a flat-bottomed oiled pan, and fry for about two or three minutes. The method is extremely simple, and it is fragrant and long-lasting. It has a unique flavor to eat. It is especially valuable to entertain guests with it. All my greedy comrades, why not try it? (According to the experiment, eating this flower is harmless and beneficial to digestion.)

Changzhou Food

— Yan Ye

Steamed buns: Nanxiang steamed buns have always been famous at sea, but I don't think they are good. At first, I thought that oranges would turn into trifoliate oranges when they crossed the Huai River. On a Sunday holiday, I rushed to Nanxiang to try them, but they were not that great. Because I am used to eating our Changzhou steamed buns, I feel that all the steamed buns in the world are tasteless. (Too exaggerated, right?) Our Changzhou steamed buns are similar in style to Nanxiang, but slightly smaller. However, the skin is thinner, and the meat filling inside is firm like a ball, not divided or scattered. There is a lot of juice outside the filling and inside the skin. The goodness of Changzhou steamed buns lies in their thin skin and juicy filling. When eating, you must first bite through the skin and suck up the juice. If you don't understand this trick, you will burn your lips and tongue with the juice, or splash it all over the table, or stain your clothes. Also, when eating, add ginger and vinegar, and you will really feel that the taste is endless. All the major tea houses in Changzhou also sell snacks, wine, and dishes. The steamed bun business is the biggest in the morning. There are two types of steamed buns, one is ordinary, as mentioned above, and the other is like crab, which can only be eaten in the autumn wind. The former sells for two copper coins each, and the latter sells for three coins, which is really a good snack that is cheap and good. Now these steamed buns have come to Shanghai. The store name is Dafeng and it is located next to the Tianchan Stage on Yunnan Road. It is run by people from Changzhou. All the chefs and waiters are also from Changzhou, so the style and taste of the steamed buns here are exactly the same as in Changzhou. Foodies may wish to try it to verify what I said. However, the price is more expensive than in Changzhou. The ordinary one sells for two cents of foreign money, and the crab one costs five cents. This is because all the expenses at sea are much higher than in Changzhou, so it has to be. But after you eat it, you will still say that it is good value for money. The second is rice wine. The rice wine dumpling shops in Shanghai must add the words Changzhou to their signs, which shows that Changzhou rice wine is very famous. However, in our Changzhou area, there is no one who praises rice wine. Changzhou also does not see any shops that specialize in selling rice wine dumplings. Although small hotels also sell rice wine as an accompaniment, only women and children who cannot drink occasionally go to buy some to eat and play. Changzhou is not known for its rice wine, but rice wine shops at sea must add the words Changzhou, which really makes me wonder. The third is sesame cake: Shanghai's flatbread is like our Changzhou sesame cake. Some people in Shanghai disdain to mention flatbread, but people who eat Changzhou sesame cake will praise it endlessly. This sesame cake is made in the same way as flatbread, but it is incredibly crispy and melts in your mouth like chewing on a cake. The sweet ones are filled with lard and white sugar, and the salty ones are made with lard and salt. Eating one in the morning is enough to fill your stomach. Many large tea houses have them and sell them as snacks with steamed buns. Deng Zhao, the former president of Suzhou Advanced Industrial School, who studied abroad, ate it once in Chang and praised the beauty of Changzhou sesame cake whenever he met someone, which shows that what I said is true. However, it must be eaten as soon as it is made, and it is tasteless when cold, so it must be made to order and there is no ready-made one for sale.

Securities

"New Measures" Fuel Bond Market Surge

Yesterday, at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, the market atmosphere was extremely tense. Amid the highly critical situation in Tianjin and Beijing, the bond market suddenly experienced a rapid rise. The northern syndicate was aggressively buying to cover short positions, while those with floating short positions felt particularly panicked and followed the trend, groping forward in the dark. Although it was reported that areas such as Miyun and Tangshan had been abandoned and the threat to Tianjin and Beijing was imminent, it was also said that Huang Fu had entered Beijing to implement so-called new measures for the situation in North China. As a result, market prices advanced rapidly with a strong upward trend. The opening price in the morning session rose by 70 to 80 cents. At that time, it was rumored in the market that the Japanese had declared the Great Wall as the boundary and would not invade Tianjin and Beijing, so there was hope that Tianjin and Beijing would be spared. The northern syndicate was most aggressive in covering short positions, and the second session rose by another 50 to 60 cents. In the afternoon, rumors of the so-called new measures became widespread, and investor sentiment became more bullish. The opening price rose by another 60 to 70 cents. The strength of the upward trend and the favorable situation were unprecedented. At the close, some temporary bulls cashed out, resulting in a pullback, with prices falling by as much as 60 to 70 cents. However, some types of bonds still rose by 10 to 20 cents. The sudden arrival of such important news as the settlement date approached made the surge even more powerful. As a result, market prices rose across the board, ranging from 60 cents to 1.7 yuan. The total trading volume was 15,777,000 yuan, including 20,000 yuan in cash, 6,910,000 yuan in futures for salt and tobacco tax, 2,385,000 yuan in futures for demobilization bonds, 2,310,000 yuan in futures for the 1929 Lan-Shan bonds, and 3,295,000 yuan in futures for the 1920 customs bonds. The remaining amounts ranged from tens of thousands to 850,000 yuan.

Lower American Cotton Prices Pressure Yarn and Cotton Market

The yarn market has weakened again due to the continuous decline in American cotton prices, which has softened investor sentiment. However, major buyers are still purchasing "Jia Ma" grade yarn, while retail investors are lukewarm. The market is trending downward again. While the market for locally produced yarn is gradually developing in the South China region, demand from other areas remains sluggish. Rumors are rampant in the market, claiming that factories are uniting to push prices up. However, the current critical situation and economic hardship are hindering the yarn market's upward momentum.

Selling Spree Sweeps Flour and Wheat Market

The flour market: After the opening bell in the morning, the price of all months declined unanimously. The quoted price for foreign wheat fell again by about two tenths of a yuan. The domestic situation became increasingly treacherous. The situation in the Tianjin and Beiping area became more chaotic by the day and seemed to be on the verge of collapse. Therefore, after the opening bell in the morning, Tianjin merchants continued to retreat step by step. Distant months also saw a decline because the new wheat harvest was approaching and a bumper harvest was expected. Both industry insiders and outsiders were unanimously selling, so the market atmosphere was weak. When the afternoon session opened, the situation in the north had become more serious. The real sales merchants adopted an extremely pessimistic attitude, which made the long positions deeply uneasy. Subsequent months also saw minor selling by large and small factories, and opening prices were also weak. Given this stable situation, if North sales were to make a decisive move, it would not be surprising for the current month to fall to 2.35 yuan. As a result, the price of the current month fell by two cents compared to the previous day, June fell by two cents and 2.5 mils, July fell by one cent and a half, August and September fell by one cent and 2.5 mils, and October fell by one cent.

The wheat market: The price of all months in both the morning and afternoon sessions continued to decline steadily. The current price decline was due to the imminent harvest of new wheat in the country. The factories, because of the new wheat season, still had a large amount of foreign wheat available for production and were not paying attention to the new wheat. In recent days, the situation in the north has been such that flour sales would inevitably be affected, and the wheat market became even more hopeless. Therefore, the selling pressure was extremely strong in both the morning and afternoon sessions, and prices fell frequently. As a result, the price of July fell by four cents compared to the previous day, August and September fell by five cents, and October fell by six cents.

Foreign Rice and Xian Rice Sell Very Well

Yesterday, Fuzhou merchants were very greedy and actively purchased Xianggan Rice and Xian Rice in the market. They also purchased small amounts of Foreign Rice, as well as newly arrived Xian Rice from Wuhu, Nanjing, and Jiangbei. The total transaction volume in the city was about 8,000 bags, which helped to support the declining market. The inventory in the market is still sufficient. In addition to Xian Rice from various routes, the inventory of Foreign Rice is even larger. Recently, the Shanghai market has been lively, and the supply is continuous. In addition to Xianggan, Du Jian Xian Rice from this province and various Xian Rice from Anhui have also arrived. The weather is hot, and local sales are weak. Stockpilers are planning to sell. Even merchants on this street intend to sell. Due to the hot weather, cargo owners are seeking to sell quickly, and the market is trending downward. Yesterday, the Min merchants were very greedy. In addition to Wenzhou merchants purchasing more than 200 bags of Hunan Ji Jing Rice, it was all purchased by the Min merchants. The local merchants did not purchase it and returned 1,500 bags of purchased Xiaojiao Rice to the Min merchants. The price of all rice was the same as the previous session, without any changes, it was said.

News on Silk, Tea, and the Silkworm Season in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

(Rugao) Also a silkworm breeding area in Jiangsu, farmers in Chahe, Dingyan, Juegang, Shuangdian, Youfangtou, Matang, Baipu, Libao, and other areas pay great attention to silkworm breeding. In recent years, due to unfavorable weather, silkworm cocoons have repeatedly failed, and the cost of silkworm breeding has been completely lost. The rural economy has collapsed. This year, silkworm farmers are borrowing money to breed silkworms. However, borrowing is difficult, and silkworm rearing is not smooth. Those who hatched local varieties early account for 40%, while those who breed foreign varieties later are more numerous. The weather is warm, and the silkworm larvae are developing smoothly. The early batches have already completed their third sleep and abandoned the leaves, while the second batch is entering their third sleep, and the late batches are only starting their second sleep. The current situation is very good.

(Changxing) Farmers, in light of the continuous poor harvests of silkworm cocoons, are considering economic depression. This year, silkworm farmers are facing financial difficulties and are borrowing money from the local township office to raise silkworms. Many farmers in Baifubu, Hongxingqiao, Niudianqiao, Xucangqiao, Heping, Lincheng, Xiayuanyuan, and Si'an are hatching improved varieties. The climate is warm, and the silkworm larvae hatch evenly and develop well. The early batches are about to enter their third sleep, while the second batch is abandoning the leaves after the second sleep, and the late batches are only in their second sleep. Mulberry leaf production is abundant, exceeding demand, and the price of leaves is only 30 to 40 cents per hundred catties. The other day, there was thunder and rain all night, but fortunately the silkworm larvae were still young and there was little impact.

Sichuan Raw Silk Sales Are Still Not Quiet

▲The price of white factory raw silk is small, and the cost is high… It is difficult to sell Jili raw silk due to a shortage.▲

Yesterday, in the local foreign firm silk market, the sales of Sichuan raw silk from Zhou factories were still not quiet. The cost of white factory raw silk was high, and the price was small, so the factories were waiting and watching. The inventory of Jili raw silk was thin, and transactions were difficult to facilitate. A Collection of Recent News from Wuyuan Tea

(New Tea Estimated to Lose Money) The mountain farmers in the four villages of Wuyi County have been harvesting tea for weeks, but due to the cold weather, the tea buds are difficult to sprout and develop, and the daily output is small. In previous years, after six or seven days of harvesting and processing, at least half of the harvest was achieved. At the moment, the new tea produced by each household has not reached 40% of the total output. According to the tea farmers' estimates, this year's tea production will vary, with some being similar to last year, some being 70-80% as usual, and some even having a 50% shortfall. The reason is that the weather is not warm, and the tea leaves are tender and difficult to pick, so it is inevitable to lose money. In summary, the tea production in the whole county this year is mixed, and there is definitely a decrease compared to previous years.

(Mountain Farmers Secretly Complain) The poor farmers in this county have no land to cultivate themselves. All of their annual household expenses depend on the income from tea sales. This year's tea production is generally poor, and the cost of labor, food, firewood, and charcoal has not decreased compared to the past. The tea shops, suffering from last year's losses, are generally lowering the mountain prices by 20-30 yuan this year. Losing money on tea and losing money on prices, being exploited on both sides, one often sees mountain farmers picking tea under the tea trees, all hanging their heads and secretly complaining.

(Tea Shops' Finances Still Closed) The tea shops stationed in the tea-producing areas used to be keen to attract loans and foreign exchange, but in recent years, a small number of speculative tea shops have failed to control the shops, and in light of the huge losses suffered by the tea shops last year, the tea market has not improved this year, and the financial sources are not smooth. They have all shifted their focus, tightened lending. The reporter recently asked a manager of a certain shop about the business policy this year. He immediately replied without hesitation that the purpose of this year is not to accept customers, and the shops are free to deposit tea at will. The shop's attitude of fatigue and the tightening of lending can be seen from this.

(Tea Shops Opening One After Another) Most of the tea shops in the four villages of this county are solid, but there are also quite a few tea shops that are engaged in speculation without capital. Last year, all the shops suffered universal losses. This year, the original wealthy tea shops are suffering from the depletion of old funds, and it is difficult to raise new funds quickly. Facing this financial closure, it is really a lot of careful planning. Therefore, two weeks ago, there were still very few shops planning to open. Unexpectedly, this week, the new tea picking has started, and the traders who were determined not to talk about the tea business could not help but get excited. In recent days, whether they are wealthy or non-wealthy, new or old tea shops, about 80% of them have been preparing to open their scales, and it seems that they are still continuing to work hard in their business. However, it remains to be seen whether a small number of speculative tea shops can all open their doors, depending on whether or not they can raise funds. At this time, they are just clamoring and joining in the fun.

(Future Prediction of Mountain Prices) The mountain price is related to the cost of boxed tea. In the past ten years, due to the competition among tea shops and the rise in prices, the cost of labor, food, and expenses for mountain farmers has been increasing, from 30 yuan per load to 90 yuan. In the past few years, the tea shops have not been defeated, so in order to compete for new tea mountain prices, they did not have time to consider the price, and they all bought at the same price. Last year, they learned the lesson of heavy capital losses, and this year they cannot help but consider the competition of high and low mountain prices. The shops have recently declared verbally that they will all lower the mountain prices, with some saying that they will offer 30 yuan per load, or 100 yuan for three loads, and some saying that the most they will offer is 40 yuan. If this limit is violated, they will not take a single leaf. Although that is what they say, I don't know whether the mountain farmers who are the owners of the goods will be able to agree to them. According to the reporter's speculation, the price will be around 50 yuan when the scale is opened in the future.

Ten Raw Silk Tea Farms' Precious Eyebrow Tea Sales Increase in Europe

Commentary

Scabies and Tuberculosis

—Xiaozi

丨To Prove That China Will Not Perish丨

In recent days, news reports indicate that the situation in North China is becoming increasingly tense. Those who are concerned about the country have more material for deep discussions. Therefore, some people say, "The abandonment of Rehe, the loss of various ports, the fall of Dolon, and the recent attempt by the enemy to seize west of the Luan River, as well as the aircraft demonstrating towards Tianjin and Beijing, are all due to the inaction of the authorities, who are unwilling to divert some of the forces suppressing bandits to resist Japan. Otherwise, the enemy would not dare to be so rampant."

However, this is ultimately the talk of old fogies, so pedantic as to be unworthy of mention. How could China perish? This gentleman has not studied geometry, so he does not understand the principle that "If angle A equals angle B, and angle B equals angle C, then angle A must also equal angle C." Of course, he also would not know that "To resist foreign aggression, one must first pacify the interior," and even less would he know the profound truth that "Pacifying the interior is resisting foreign aggression!" However, old fogies always pride themselves on their age and do not submit to those who do not accept old age. Therefore, I need to explain and provide detailed evidence.

China! Remember, only China! Currently, there are two enemies. One is the "imperialists," so it is said that we must have an "anti-imperialist" war. The other enemy is China's mortal enemy, which is said to be ten, hundred, thousand, million times more harmful to China than the "imperialist enemy" (this is a fabrication). This enemy is surnamed "Red" and is also named "imperialist." Its alias is "Communist bandit," so we also have wars to "kill Communists" and "suppress bandits." However, the "imperialist enemy" is an external enemy, while the "Communist bandit" is an internal enemy. Therefore, the "Communist bandit" is, of course, much more serious than the "imperialist enemy." For example, if someone suffers from skin diseases such as sores and boils, while another person suffers from heart disease or tuberculosis, soon the person suffering from heart disease or tuberculosis will kick the bucket because it is difficult to treat. The friend with the sores and boils will happily eat steamed dates with lard every day. At most, he will only cut away the rotten flesh or discard a layer of skin. His life will definitely not be ended because of this. To give another example, if you use a small knife to cut off a corner of a plump and delicious pear, even if the skin and flesh change color after a while, it will definitely not breed maggots. But if a chemical reaction occurs inside the core and it rots from the core outward, then there is no cure. Therefore, the "Communist bandit" is like heart disease or tuberculosis, and also like the maggots that cause the core of the pear to rot. If we want to preserve China's old life, we must fundamentally treat it, and it is not enough to capture and trample the "maggots" one by one. As for the "imperialist enemy," it does not matter much, like having scabies, we only need to "cut off" the skin with sores and eat some "steamed dates with lard" and the like.

In recent days, although it is said that the Japanese army is approaching and North China is becoming more dangerous, that is not important. Because the same newspaper also publishes in the same typeface the news of the successive victories of the "bandit suppression" military and the recapture of "bandit" areas and the capture of "bandit" leaders. Is this news not a joyous, astonishing, and even maddening fact that China will definitely not perish?

Moreover, "bandit suppression" also has a side effect, which is a powerful demonstration against the "imperialist enemy." That is to say, don't mess around, I have troops. If you don't believe it, I'll show you!

Old fogies, have you cleared your clogged mind yet?

Redemption of Pawned Goods

— Wen Bing

Friends who have been circling back from the accounting office of the newspaper or the counter of the bookstore are mostly clutching their pockets tightly, revealing an unusually excited look. They shrink three steps into two, first striding into the dance hall or the cinema. Then, in the hazy twilight, one can see the thin, elongated shadows of these people reflected in front of the fortress-like pawnshop.

For some reason, the chains of economics, one shackle after another, have bound me. So, on an evening at the end of last month, I, like a petty thief, stealthily and nervously walked to the pawnshop counter that was taller than my head. My ears and cheeks turned red and then green, burning hot. My eyes were also blurred, and I only saw the room spinning. The iron bars that were mounted on the counter seemed to fall one by one on my forehead, causing a bone-piercing pain. In my dazed consciousness, I received the money and rushed back in one breath, lying on the bed, my hands full of cold sweat, my heart pounding.

In theory, I shouldn't be in such an awkward situation. After years of wandering life, entering the pawnshop should be as common as a regular meal, shouldn't it? I should have some experience. Moreover, now that I still have this life and can still go in and out of the pawnshop, in today's China, I can still boast that I am a "quasi-lucky guy." Moreover, even Mr. Lu Xun, the current authority in the literary world, has experienced such a period of life, so what does it matter?

However, I always feel uneasy, as if I have lost my soul.

It was the day before yesterday. I walked out of the newspaper office happily. Passing by the dance hall, my heart felt a little panicked. My consciousness immediately told me that this was not a place you needed to go. Moreover, you haven't had any experience, so how could you go in? Passing by the cinema, I happened to see the screening of a domestically produced masterpiece that was all the rage and had even participated in the Italian International Film Exhibition! The feet of this metropolitan dweller no longer moved forward, so I stopped there.

Coming out of the cinema, according to the usual procedure, I should go to the pawnshop. However, although it was already five o'clock, the sun was still hanging obliquely in the western sky. Experience told me that going to the pawnshop at this time, even if it was to redeem something, my ears and cheeks would still turn red and green. The most annoying thing was that those passersby often glanced at you irrelevantly. I circled around for a long time before the night gradually unfolded. So I went up with an excited heart. Firstly, redeeming something is a relatively honorable thing, and secondly, this time I was able to redeem it in less than a month, which clearly indicated that my life was improving. I remember that the clothes and pants that I pawned in a pawnshop in Zhabei in the winter of the year before last, after the artillery fire of the "January 28th" incident, when I went to inquire about them in April last year, even the pawnshop was gone, which was really annoying. I placed the money on the high counter and called out "Redeem." A greasy fat face appeared inside the iron bars. But I was not embarrassed at all. In the five minutes that I stood waiting, I was the only one redeeming something, but the space under the high counter was crowded with customers, and people were still pouring in at the door, men, women, old, young, tall, short, rickshaw pullers, young men in suits, poorly dressed poor women, and fashionable girls in cheongsams and leather shoes, each with an unstable soul and an unstable look, staring at the greasy fat face inside the iron bars. "This business is really good!" I praised silently. Suddenly, an old hunched woman appeared at the door. "That is a true pauper!" I turned and thought to myself. "Four jiao and six fen of interest!" I suddenly turned my eyes to look at the sign that read "Monthly interest of one fen and eight li," and couldn't help but blurt out, "This is where high-interest loans are exploited!"

"That is a true pauper!" "Four jiao and six fen of interest!" "Monthly interest of one fen and eight li!" "This is where high-interest loans are exploited!" On the way home, I kept repeating these words, as if a dilapidated social scene was playing before my eyes.

Poem Composed After Chancing to See Mr. He Jiamenglu's Rubbing of a Buddhist Bell Cast by the Buddhist Association to Commemorate the Japanese Earthquake; Rhyming with His Original Poem, At a Time When Rehe Had Been Lost and There Were News of Several Treaty Ports Not Being Defended

— Lü Mengjiao

The turbulent waves surged from the east, Heaven sent disaster to the Central Plains, Alas, the inner regions have all fallen, Worms, sand, apes, and cranes are crushed.

………………

Even if the war leaves half of us wounded, Innocent lives are still harmed, The ancient Arong all evoke the same sigh, Who will comfort the heroic souls on the battlefield?

………………

Don't say that the national law has lost Qin's harshness, Praise and blame are too vague and obscure, What does compensation for land amount to in the present situation? The azure sky no longer holds thunder and lightning.

The sound of the bell cannot dispel the fierce ghosts, The border regions still echo with war drums and horns, Who can stop the enemy at the mighty pass? Let future generations continue the glorious achievements of the past.

Exterior Scene of Pingcheng

A Visit to the Second Jiangsu Prison

— Tinghua

Every graduating class of the Law Department of our school (China Public School) visits not only the courts in various districts but also various prisons for practical study and research. The other day (the 14th), along with classmates Jiang Zhanggen, Wen Bing, and others, a group of forty-six people led by Professor Yang of our school went to Caohejing to visit the Second Jiangsu Prison. That morning at nine o'clock, we gathered at the school on Route Tenant in the French Concession and hired several large cars, which took us directly to our destination. We first entered the reception room, where the warden of the prison, Tian Zhongfu, gave a talk. He said briefly that the prison has about 1,800 inmates, including 1,500 criminal offenders and 300 military offenders. Most of the criminal offenders are sent by the local courts, while the military offenders are sent by the garrison headquarters and the security department. The food rations and treatment for criminal offenders and military offenders are different. The daily cost per person for criminal offenders is one jiao, and for military offenders, it is one jiao and five fen. The reason for the difference is that the Ministry of the Army, the Economic School, and the Ministry of Justice are more affluent. In addition, there are two foreign offenders, whose food rations cost three jiao per person per day. The preferential treatment for foreign offenders is the same in all countries. He (Tian, referring to himself) had previously held prison positions in Harbin and other places. He had only taken over here for four or five months. Regarding military offenders, this place has always advocated leniency. However, if their words and actions are too loud and unrestrained, their freedom has been slightly restricted recently, so these people inevitably have many complaints. We then visited the prison cells. The cells were specially built in a gear shape. One room at the axle of the gear is like a pavilion, with eight sides. One side is a corridor, and the remaining seven are labeled A, B, C, D, E, F, and G, each connected to more than a dozen prison cells. The guards can see all the alleyways of the cells from the center by looking around, which is the reason for such construction, for easy management of the prisoners. (1) Block A, with dozens of cells, is for military offenders and was not convenient to visit. (2) Most of the doors of the dozens of cells in Block B were open. Each door had a number (prisoners are not identified by name but by a number). There were at least eight and at most twelve people in each cell. At the end of the cell alley was the First Workshop, which was the rope-making section and the box-pasting section. The prisoners were all working, half making zongzi ropes and half pasting matchboxes. The managers supervised them, just like in an ordinary workshop. (3) The houses in Blocks C to G were constructed similarly, but the workshops at the end of the cell alleys were different. For example, the end of the alley in Block C was called the Second Workshop, which was a printing house. Typesetters, printers, and bookbinders were all working there without any sign of fatigue. (4) The end of the alley in Block D was the education hall, which had a sewing section and a wool-picking section. The prisoners were all sitting quietly in the education hall and were not seen working. (5) The end of the alley in Block E was the Third Workshop, which was the knitting section, i.e., making socks; the Fourth Workshop was the box-pasting section, i.e., pasting matchboxes; and the Fifth Workshop was the weaving section. The prisoners were all working and seemed quite skilled. (6) The end of the alley in Block F was the Sixth Workshop, which was the yarn-reeling section and the bamboo and wood section, with nothing particularly special. We then went to visit the women's prison. That day, there were a total of 142 female inmates, most of whom were making white bamboo cloth handkerchiefs, and some were making children's clothes and lace, as if it were a women's vocational training center. Judging by their expressions, they seemed to have forgotten that they were in prison. (7) The infirmary had an examination room and equipment such as medicines. (8) The kitchen was where food and drink were prepared for the inmates. The rice and vegetables were, of course, rough and simple and could not be compared with those of ordinary people, but they were still clean and fresh, and attention was paid to hygiene. There were also barbering and bathing sections, but we did not have time to visit them before returning, it was said.

Frog Sounds

— Qiong

The nanny left, leaving a baby just over a year old crying in my arms. To make the baby quiet for a while, I held him and wandered in the countryside near the city.

It was dusk at this time. Spring had not completely left, and everything still retained the vitality of youth. I wandered here, and I temporarily felt satisfied with this illusory life. The strangest thing was that the baby stopped crying at this time and quietly listened to the noisy frog sounds around him, and later even fell asleep on my shoulder.

Ah! These frog sounds, I began to understand the beauty of these frog sounds. But this caused my desolate homesickness and the melancholy of past events.

I remember at this time five years ago, our group of officer political school classmates was setting off for the countryside for field training. We killed, we charged, we ran between the mountains, we rested in the vast plains. We held a short carbine in our hands, and we carried bullets on our backs. Whenever we were tired and sleepy, we listened quietly to the war drum-like frog sounds. In their songs, the power of youthful and vigorous life flowed throughout. But we were very cruel after all. Several times we caught several small frogs that had not even shed their tails and conveniently executed them, because the destruction of this small life would not leave any traces in my personal heart, at least. Indeed, at that time I flaunted my youth, and I was determined to gather the greatest strength to break through the dark encirclement. I wanted to seek liberation for myself, and I longed for the light of the future. I entrusted my life to this carbine, and I aimed at imperialism and all enemies.

However, this life of "power" finally flowed away gently like a dream. Everything five years ago is now just an empty memory. Now, what I am holding in my hands is not a carbine but a baby. I have become

Page 19

the mother of this new life. My career, my future, I entrust to this child. I am almost... what? Ah! A virtuous wife and good mother!

Shopkeeper Communications

Land Requisition

Editor:

Recently, our Xiangshan County is planning to build a motor road. The route has already been surveyed and will start construction soon. Yesterday, I received a letter from home saying that this road will cut across my five-mu field.

Sir, of course, I cannot oppose this matter, but does this mean that my five-mu field will be sacrificed? Please give me an explanation. I respectfully ask,

Zhang Naiwen, Ze'an

××××

Editor's Note: According to the current laws of our country, the government, in order to build roads or other public buildings, may, when necessary, requisition land from the people. The owners of the land being requisitioned may not resist, so Mr. Zhang cannot oppose this matter at all.

As for the requisition of land, it does not mean that it can be occupied casually. The government should determine the land price with reference to local conditions. Therefore, Mr. Zhang's land, after being requisitioned, can obtain a corresponding price. However, this price is estimated by the government and cannot be bargained by you. Speaking of the payment of this land price, some are paid in cash at once, and some are paid in installments, which is uncertain, but the government must have a clear indication in advance, and all households are treated equally, without distinction.

After your five-mu field is used to build the road, it probably won't be completely gone. The remaining field is still yours; the government absolutely cannot circle a fraction more than what is needed for building the road. Conversely, you cannot force the government to buy the field that is left over after the road construction. However, if the field that is left over is less than one fen and is not connected to your other fields, then if you are willing, the government should buy it all together at a price. The principle of land requisition is nothing more than this; as for the detailed rules, they vary from place to place, but they cannot violate this principle.

Fiction

The Life of the Five Beauties (10) (Continued)

— Ling He

However, even so, Miss Liu could still enjoy some leisure: this was very clear to Wu Gui. For example, Master Zhang earned five yuan a month in Shanghai and sent it home, and he also had many savings in Beijing that could be withdrawn at any time. So Miss Liu was also happy. She could buy several sets of fashionable clothes every month. Wu Gui took care of everything inside and outside (the reason she brought Wu Gui here was for this), and she could listen to operas, play cards, and even play the erhu and sing a few lines when she was happy. Everyone in the neighborhood envied her for having accumulated so much merit in her previous life, so that she could enjoy such good fortune in this life.

But soon she gradually became bored. What made her most angry was the time when a steward was suddenly sent back from his post and broke into her room in the middle of the night. Later, according to Wu Gui's guess, it was probably the First Madam who intentionally instructed him to do this to see if she was doing anything bad. This made her unhappy for several days. Sometimes she was determined to sneak out with a wild man to vent her anger, but she couldn't muster up that kind of interest for a while and hadn't done it until now.

Today, she was casually holding a novel, lying lazily on the bed. In the middle of reading, she suddenly came across these two sentences:

"… You are living in happiness, but you are not aware of it and are tired of happiness…"

So she gently closed the book and closed her eyes as if she was lost in thought.

The spring sunlight was blown into the window by the cool breeze, ironing on her face, and leaving two shallow tear marks at the corners of her eyes.

(10) Now She Belongs To Our People

God's tricks on people are often both funny and sad. For example, now that Miss Liu had married into the Zhang family, she should have continued to live in a peaceful and simple time, but God's intention was not like that. Master Zhang happened to die when his official career was at its peak. Moreover, he died very strangely. It was said that he didn't have any serious illness, but he just had a boil on his back that caused him to writhe in pain for three days and three nights before kicking the bucket and dying. He didn't even have time to give good instructions for his funeral, only instructing Miss Liu that she must remarry.

According to the old masters who had reached a certain age, this kind of death was because the underworld used a weighing hook to hook his spine, and it was inevitable for someone who was not honest as an official to die like this. However, it was not always the case. As Wu Gui, my brother, said, who could go to the underworld to take a trip? Who had seen it? Moreover, although Master Zhang was a little corrupt, he may not have harmed anyone's life. How many officials looted, but not one of them died clean. So no one can figure out God's affairs.

However, our Miss Liu was now divorced from the Zhang family. First, the First Madam never liked such a... Her heart thought:

"Oh! Don't bother, who can take care of so much?"

Outside it was still raining, depressing rain. She thought deeply without a clue, and she herself was a little unsure; why had it suddenly become like this?
